消息 221

本埠安納昌路三二三號元昌廣告公司廣擴電臺爲出版全部姊妹花播音劇本。特擴大宣傳。曾在全滬華商電臺作空前盛舉。播送是書作者李昌艦君聞聲戲循環特别節目。並於播送特别節目時。先行發售預約。全書計三十萬字。定價八角。預約僅售四角八分。並加贈李昌鑑君親筆簽名照片及對聯一付。茲已全書印竣。開始發售。有盡家倪絅賢君之外封面。楊藝星君之内封面。本月底前仍售特價七角二分。尙有普及本實售五角四分云。

啟事　本刊因篇幅狹小，各團體節目未能儘盡刊登　且發稿時間關係，遺漏諸多，特此啟事，並致歉意。

播音節目編輯室

1934.10.22

Various Yuan and Ministry Departments Rush to Prepare Work Reports 1

Representatives from Various Regions Arrive in Beijing to Attend

Railway Department Formulates Precautionary Measures

(Nanjing) The work reports of various Yuan and Ministry departments for the Fifth National Congress have been submitted to the National Government one after another, and are being organized by the Civil Service Office for presentation at the Congress. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) In anticipation of the imminent opening of the Fifth National Congress and the arrival of central committee representatives from various regions in Nanjing, the Railway Department has formulated precautionary measures to ensure safety. These measures have been circulated to all railway administration bureaus for compliance. 1. Section chiefs and police officers are responsible for protecting station platforms and key locations. 2. Ticketless travel is prohibited. 3. Patrol officers and detectives accompanying trains must maintain close contact with the military police escorting the trains. 4. Any suspicious individuals on board must be thoroughly questioned, and tea servers are instructed to be vigilant at all times. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Political work reports submitted by various agencies to the Fifth National Congress have been compiled and sent to the National Government for forwarding to the Central Government. These include reports from the Judicial Yuan, the National Economic Council, and the Western Capital Construction Committee. Other agencies are also rushing to complete and submit their reports. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The Kuomintang branch in Shantou has selected Wu Zifang, Zheng Junying, and Liang Shutong as representatives to the Fifth National Congress. They will depart for Beijing at the end of the month. (21st Dispatch)

Umezu Inspects Japanese Troops Along the Beining Railway Line 2

Returns to Tianjin from Beiping, Then Proceeds to Tanggu

Japanese Troops in Beiping and Tianjin Conduct Separate Drills

(Beiping) The commander of the Japanese garrison in Tianjin, Umezu, completed his inspection of Japanese troops in Beiping and returned to Tianjin this morning. After a brief rest, he proceeded to Tanggu, Tangshan, Yuguan, and other locations to inspect the Japanese garrison along the Beining Railway Line. He will then return to Tianjin. (21st Dispatch)

(Tianjin) This morning at 8:00 AM, over two hundred Japanese soldiers, including infantry, artillery, and cavalry, conducted street fighting drills in the Japanese concession. The communications battalion was also deployed, testing communications on Awaji Street and Flower Garden Street. Traffic was blocked on Akashi Street and Suma Street. Japanese soldiers were stationed along the streets to guard the area. The drills concluded at 12:00 PM. This afternoon, Japanese commander Umezu returned to Tianjin from Beiping after inspecting the garrison and then proceeded to Tanggu and Tangshan for further inspections. (21st Dispatch)

(Beiping) Seventeen fully armed Japanese soldiers arrived in Beiping this morning. After disembarking, they proceeded to the Tan Guobing Barracks. (21st Dispatch)

(Beiping) Several dozen Japanese soldiers stationed in Beiping carried rifles, pistols, and machine guns this morning and conducted live-fire exercises in batches at Miaojia Di in the eastern suburbs. They returned to the city in the afternoon. (21st Dispatch)

Hebei Provincial Administrative Conference Proposals Classified Into Five Categories 3

Group Discussions Will Be Held After the Opening

Attending Personnel and Experts Report Their Arrival

(Tianjin) Proposals for the Hebei Provincial Administrative Conference have been classified into five categories and will be discussed starting on the afternoon of the 25th: 1. Maintaining public security throughout the province; 2. Rural relief; 3. Improving administration in various counties; 4. Reorganizing land taxes throughout the province; 5. Developing industries throughout the province. Civil Affairs Director Wei Jian will preside over the conference. Yin Rugeng and Tao Shangming, commissioners of the Ji, Mi, Luan, and Yu administrative districts, will also attend and participate in the discussions. They are expected to arrive in Tianjin from Beiping on the evening of the 24th. (21st Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Attending personnel and experts for the Hebei Provincial Administrative Conference have reported their arrival, totaling over 110 people. The secretariat received another twenty proposals from various parties today. The conference will open on the morning of the 25th, and group discussions will be held in the afternoon to review proposals related to civil affairs, education, industry, finance, and construction separately. Discussions will begin on the 26th. (21st Dispatch)

(Beiping) The first Hebei Provincial Administrative Conference has been scheduled to be held in Tianjin on the 25th of this month for a period of five days. The various departments and counties have submitted three to four hundred proposals. In addition to the provincial committee and department directors, over forty county magistrates from across the province will attend. Tao Shangming and Yin Rugeng, administrative commissioners of the Luan, Yu, Ji, and Mi districts, will also participate. Key issues to be discussed at this conference include consolidating public security throughout the province and rural relief. The issue of eliminating excessive and miscellaneous taxes will also be discussed in detail. The Luan, Yu, Ji, and Mi districts have each nominated two county magistrates to attend, namely the magistrates of Leting and Funing counties for the Luan, Yu district, and the magistrates of Sanhe and Shunyi counties for the Ji, Mi district. (21st Dispatch)

(Beiping) Tao Shangming arrived in Beiping last night from Tianjin. According to him, he will leave Beiping on the 24th to return to Tianjin to attend the Hebei Provincial Government Administrative Conference. Various counties have submitted proposals, and most county magistrates will arrive to attend. Civil Affairs Director Wei Jian will represent the chairman at the conference. Although there are bandits in the Luan, Yu district, the situation is not as severe as rumored. However, the constant rumors are causing public panic. He plans to pay a visit to Director Huang tomorrow to report on everything. (20th Dispatch)

British Ambassador Cadogan Plans to Inspect Southern China 4

(Nanjing) According to information from the British Consulate, British Ambassador Cadogan is scheduled to travel south on the Beiping-Shanghai through train on the 23rd, accompanied by his secretary Ashton. He will arrive in Nanjing on the evening of the 24th and plans to stay in Nanjing for two weeks to meet with Acting Foreign Minister Wang. He will then travel to Shanghai at the beginning of next month. Having been in China for six months, he has not yet inspected Southern China. He is scheduled to depart from Shanghai on the 12th of next month aboard the British warship HMS "Moths" for a tour of the southeastern coastal areas, first visiting Fuzhou, then Xiamen on the 17th, Shantou on the 20th, and Guangzhou on the 22nd. He will return to Hong Kong on the 25th and back to Shanghai on the 30th. On December 10th, he will take the Beiping-Shanghai through train directly back to Beiping. During these two months, the embassy's affairs in Beiping will be handled by Counselor Evey. (21st Dispatch)

(Beiping) British Ambassador Cadogan is scheduled to depart for Shanghai and then Hong Kong on the 23rd to inspect the recent situation of overseas Chinese merchants in Southern China. The round trip to Guangzhou, Shantou, and other places is expected to take three weeks before returning to Beiping. Counselor Teichman of the British Embassy, on a mission from Cadogan, is scheduled to visit Nanjing on the 22nd to meet with our longstanding authorities to discuss matters. (21st Dispatch)

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Tours the Maoling and Zhouling Tombs in Shaanxi 5

Receives Graduates of Military Academy

Hosts Banquet for Shao and Yang Couple

(Xi'an) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, accompanied by his wife Madame Soong Mei-ling, Deputy Commander Zhang, Secretary-General Yang, and escorted by the Shao and Yang couple, departed by car from the provincial capital at 9:30 AM on the 21st to tour the Maoling and Zhouling tombs. They returned to the provincial capital at 4:00 PM and rested at the New City Building Headquarters. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Xi'an) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek summoned Cao Guohua and other graduates of the Central Military Academy's senior education class at 9:00 AM on the 21st. He also received Qi Jingxin, director of the forestry department of the agricultural and forestry college, Supervisory Commissioner Yan Zhuang, and Military Affairs Commission Councilor Han Zhenhua, offering them encouragement. At 9:30 AM, he visited the Maoling and Zhouling tombs. In the afternoon, he returned to the province and hosted a banquet at the headquarters to entertain Shao Lizi, Yang Hucheng, and their spouses, as well as Feng Qinzhai. Deputy Commander Zhang and Secretary-General Yang were also invited to accompany them, serving as a farewell conversation. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Xi'an) Chiang Kai-shek visited Maoling Elementary School on the 21st and expressed great admiration, suggesting further expansion. He also visited the tombs of King Wen and King Wu of Zhou, as well as the tomb of the Duke of Zhou. He instructed Shao to repair the houses in front of the tombs and promised to donate funds. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Xi'an) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek ordered the Shaanxi provincial government to implement ten initiatives, including road construction, the establishment of an electrical plant, the protection of goods, and the care of livestock. The Shaanxi provincial government ordered the relevant authorities to promptly comply on the 21st. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Remnant Bandits Between Ruijin and Huichang Prepare to Break Through 6

The Army is Stationed in Hetian Bandit Area, Supplies Completely Cut Off

Chiang Ting-wen Travels Between Longyan and Xinxing to Handle Official Business

Tingzhou City Can Be Captured By The End Of This Month 7

(Fuzhou) Military sources report that 50,000 to 60,000 remnant bandits are currently gathered between Ruijin, Gucheng, and Huichang, and are planning to break through and escape. There are no longer any main bandit forces in Changting, and the direct assault on Tingzhou and Ruijin has begun. (20th Dispatch)

(Xiamen) A person from the front lines reported that the army is stationed in Hetian, and the outposts are in Cai Fenxi, dealing with the aftermath in the recovered area and building roads. The bandit area's supplies were previously imported from the Ting River, transferred from Tingzhou to Jiangxi. After the capture of Hetian, the supply line was interrupted due to the location bordering the Ting River, completing the blockade. The bandit area's supplies are now completely cut off, which alone is enough to spell the bandits' doom. (21st Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) After our army recovered Hetian, Caifang, and other places, it actively handled local rehabilitation. The political training office of the Ninth Division established a refugee camp and reformatory in Hetian, started a Baojia training class, organized a special task force and a military postal agency, and convened representatives from various villages to discuss the establishment of village offices and a district clearing committee, all of which have been established in succession. Many refugees have returned to their villages, deeply hating the bandits. The special task force has captured several important bandits in Hetian and is currently interrogating them. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) The highest-ranking communist bandits believe that they cannot gain a foothold in Changting due to the attacks from our northeast and other armies, and are indeed preparing to break through, assault western Jiangxi, and retreat to the border between Hubei and Sichuan. The front line has been moved to the Jie Ling, the border between Ruijin and Changting, where fortifications have been erected, seemingly intending to resist there and cover the retreat. Now, the Eastern Route Army's divisions have completed their military deployment to attack Tingzhou, and Tingzhou City can be captured in one fell swoop by the end of this month. Chiang Ting-wen has been traveling by plane between Zhangzhou, Xiamen, Longyan, and Xinxing for days to handle official business, and will soon move to the front line to supervise the suppression. The blockhouses on the Pengkou-Hetian highway are expected to be completed around the 25th. Feicomm terrorists occasionally appear on the Bijiashan Mountain southwest of Jiuxian Town in Shanghang, which is the roaming ground of the 72nd Regiment of the fake 24th Division. The mountain is the intersection of the defense zones of the southeast armies. Strong units have been ordered to move in and search and suppress them. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Yin Rugeng Arrives in Beiping to Talk About the Inspection of Eastern Tombs 8

The Acceptance Period Will Be At The Beginning Of Next Month

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng returned to Beiping from Tianjin this morning. According to him, he and Chaisan inspected the Eastern Tombs. After setting off, they passed through Tongzhou, Sanhe, Malanyu, and reached the Eastern Tombs. After inspecting for a week, they went to Zunhua, stayed there briefly, and then went to Yutian and Fengrun, passing through Tangshan to Tianjin. Due to inconvenient transportation, the time was delayed for a long time. The result of the inspection is that the Eastern Tombs have been severely damaged. The Eastern Tombs used to be known as a sea of trees, but now there are only a few tree roots left. Residents still dig up tree roots for fuel. The surrounding wall is about 140 miles long and has become a ruin. If you want to repair it, it will cost about 500,000 to 600,000 yuan. The Cixi Mausoleum, Shunzhi Mausoleum, Zhaoxi Mausoleum, etc. have been completely robbed. The windows and walls of the palaces are also incomplete and chaotic. This is all due to poor storage. Now that the storage committee has been reorganized, it will be formally established after acceptance. It is expected that the acceptance matter with Chai Shang will be realized at the beginning of next month. People are being summoned in Mayu to build roads so that the acceptance can be carried out smoothly. The scattered bandits in Yutian and Zunhua can be eliminated and are not a concern. I will visit Huang to report on the inspection process and ask for specific measures for acceptance, and attend the Hebei Provincial Administrative Conference on the 24th. (21st Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Orders Investigation of Unregistered Banks in Shanghai 9

A Decision to Ban Those with Unstable Funds

(Nanjing) After the China Industrial and Commercial Bank announced its liquidation, the Ministry of Finance ordered the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau to send personnel to investigate. According to the report, the reason for the bank's liquidation was the failure of the so-called Jockey Club operation, as well as insufficient capital and poor turnover. The Ministry has previously issued a notice prohibiting banks from speculation, but the bank has resumed speculation in the business of the exchange and set up a Jockey Club, which is inappropriate. Now there are many small banks in Shanghai, absorbing deposits without any guarantee, and most of them are not registered. It has been decided to order the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau to investigate in detail the banks that have not been registered by the Ministry, order them to register, and send a letter to the Shanghai Banking Association to investigate the funds and business conditions of the unregistered banks. Those with unstable funds will be banned to avoid harming society. (21st Dispatch)

Chen Changheng Discusses the Silver Export Tax Case 10

The Cost of Imported Foreign Goods Has Increased

Various Trades Will Be Affected

(Nanjing) Economist Chen Changheng said that China's economic crisis has been serious for a long time. Because people have not felt the pain, they have mostly ignored it. Since the US government began to buy silver, China's limited silver reserves have experienced unlimited overflow. Therefore, various remedial measures have emerged, including the imposition of a silver export balancing tax. However, the imposition of silver export tax cannot prohibit the export of silver. Tax increase and export ban are two different things. The tax increase can only prohibit the unlimited export of general profiteers and speculators, and cannot stop the outflow of silver. Silver exports have already been harmful to our country, so why not directly ban silver exports? We have to review the current situation of our country. 1. Hundreds of millions of yuan of imports every year must be paid in cash and silver. 2. There are many foreign banks established in our country. Since they have absorbed a large amount of cash silver, if they want to export it at any time, the government is not convenient to forcibly prevent it. Since silver exports have been taxed, the payment of a large amount of cash silver is of course also subject to taxation. Previously, foreign rice cost four yuan per bag. At this time, it must be increased by export tax beyond four yuan. This kind of excess will inevitably be compensated by imported goods and consumers. The cost of imported foreign goods has increased, and domestic goods will inevitably increase in price. As a result, the burden of the people's purchasing power is increased. Under these circumstances, various trades are naturally affected. For example, the prices of gold, yarn, flower rice, and wheat in Shanghai have risen sharply recently, all due to the increase in silver export tax and the increase in gold prices. According to a certain person in the financial sector, the unprecedented changes in market prices recently are caused by general speculative merchants, and it is expected that it will be difficult to last. In addition, the increase in silver export tax has also caused drastic changes in the foreign exchange market. In view of this, the government has specially established a market stabilization agency to stabilize domestic finance and international exchange rates. However, this kind of organization must have a large amount of funds to be effective. As for the exchange of US dollars and Chinese silver, the United States has no definite expression, whether it agrees or not, depends on how much silver our country can exchange for US dollars. It is doubtful. If there is indeed a surplus available for exchange, why not concentrate it for safekeeping as a reserve and issue value vouchers to circulate on the market? However, judging from the government's financial resources, it is not the time yet. Therefore, the better plan to prepare for the current situation is to reorganize the currency system so that Shanghai's silver coins can flow into the mainland, and the mainland's cash will no longer be concentrated in Shanghai, creating an opportunity for export. At the same time, promote domestic goods and reduce imports. This is the method of drawing salary from the bottom of the pot. (21st Dispatch)

Yang Peng Talks About Impressions of Southwest Inspection 11

Facilities Are Perfect in Guangxi

(Nanjing) Yang Peng, Counselor of the Ministry of Justice, returned from inspecting judicial affairs in the southwestern provinces. He said that he left Beijing in June to inspect judicial affairs in Sichuan, Guizhou, Yunnan, and Guangxi. He visited no fewer than fifty important places. In Sichuan, Guizhou, and Yunnan, due to natural and man-made disasters in recent years, the provincial treasuries were in short supply, resulting in dilapidated prisons and a large number of criminal and civil offenders. Because of financial difficulties, the personnel in various offices have no spirit to do things, and cases are piling up. If no reforms are made to appease the people, the future of justice will be bleak. Guangxi has been praised as a model province due to its perfect facilities. In recent years, Chairman Huang Xuchu has strived to develop transportation in various counties and open up highways without interruption. Internal affairs can be said to have entered a bright path, so justice is also better than the three provinces mentioned above. There are very few criminal cases and not many civil cases. The equipment and management in prisons are better than those in the interior. This inspection was made to inspect the actual situation in the above-mentioned places, and can only be reported to the Ministry. As for the reform steps, the Ministry will plan them. The inspection report is being compiled and will be submitted to the Ministry for reference in future reforms. (21st Dispatch)

Loan Agreement Signed 12

(Nanjing) The Huai River Diversion Committee borrowed 4 million yuan from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund for the Huai River diversion project. The committee has agreed to sign a draft agreement. After the money is allocated, a contract will be signed. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping Public Security Bureau Holds City-Wide Inspection 13

(Beiping) The Beiping Public Security Bureau will hold a city-wide inspection week starting on the 22nd. Teams from various districts will patrol the streets, inspect pedestrians, and check household registrations. In addition, the bureau plans to implement joint police-civilian self-defense measures due to the expiration of various defense periods. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

The Righteous Army of Eastern Jilin is Active 14

(Beiping) According to news from outside the pass, after Wang Delin secretly returned to the Northeast from Hong Kong, he gathered his old troops of the Righteous Army and lurked in various counties in eastern Jilin. He once occupied the capital of Jilin Province. Wang's troops completely disarmed the Yushu County police team on the 1st of this month and occupied Daxinlitun, causing a great shock. The garrisons and puppet police in various counties in eastern Jilin revolted. After hearing the news, the Japanese army attacked from Shulan, Shuangcheng, Lalinhe, and other places. Wang's troops reoccupied the Daba Number Tun in Yushu on the 6th of this month and fought bloody battles with the Japanese and puppet troops for several days and nights. According to the Japanese side's announcement, 60 Japanese soldiers who annihilated Wang Delin's troops were killed on the south bank of Lalin City, and more than 10 were captured. From this, it can be seen that the number of Japanese soldiers annihilated was not small. (21st Dispatch)

Harbin is Overcrowded 15

(Beiping) Several armed Japanese immigrants were turned back by the local people. According to news from outside the pass, due to the repeated failures of armed immigration, Japanese immigrants could not be settled. The number of Japanese immigrants in Harbin has reached 13,414 and will break through 15,000. Recently, many Japanese immigrants have fled back from eastern Jilin, and Harbin is overcrowded. (21st Dispatch)

Bandits in Miyun Harass 16

(Beiping) A person from Miyun said that when the fake Qiangguo Army, which had fled from Zunhua, crossed the Miyun-Huai boundary, it divided into two groups and looted on a large scale, causing unbearable harassment. After the joint suppression by the Second Battalion of the Security Guard stationed and the local militia, one group fled to the northwest of Huairou, attempting to disturb the border of Chahar through Afangkou. The garrison police team intercepted them, and the bandits fled back. The militia patrolled and ambushed everywhere. They have now been scattered, and the villagers are extremely panicked. (21st Dispatch)

Chiang Orders County Magistrates in Bandit Areas to Defend to the Death 17

Martyred County Magistrates Should Be Given Preferential Treatment

(Nanchang) The headquarters announced that Chiang ordered all provinces that there are eleven clauses that should be executed in the bandit area punishment and reward regulations. Now that the remnants of the bandits are about to be wiped out, county magistrates in bandit areas should defend to the death and wait for reinforcements. If their strength is exhausted, they must die with the city and not escape alone. If the city and town are lost, military law will be enforced. The county magistrates of the lost county towns in Jiangxi, Anhui, Zhejiang, and Fujian provinces have been executed or tried in separate cases. However, county magistrates who die for the city should be given preferential treatment and reported to the National Government for commendation. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanchang) The headquarters ordered all provincial governments on the 21st that, starting this year, if there are bandit police in various counties and the county magistrates die in defense of the city, the Military Affairs Commission shall request the National Government to issue a commendation order, and grant a one-time pension of 1,000 yuan and a yearly pension of 500 yuan to the bereaved family, according to the provisional regulations on wartime pensions for the army, navy, and air force, with the rank of colonel. For the pension application process, the provincial government in charge should check the pension regulations, fill in the investigation form in detail, and issue a certificate, along with the investigation form filled in by the family of the applicant, and submit it to the headquarters for consultation and transfer to the Military Affairs Commission for approval by the National Government (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Li Zongren took a car to Hekou on the 21st to transfer back to Guangxi. Before leaving, he visited Chen Jitang, Yu Hanmou, Li Yangjing and others in Meihua Village and talked for two hours. The date of Li's return to Guangdong is undetermined. (21st Dispatch)

Current Commentary

How Can the Rectification of the Western Mongolian Border Defense Be Further Delayed? By Ji 19

Ever since Outer Mongolia, under the protection of Soviet Russia, declared independence, the situation in Inner Mongolia has been considered serious. After the September 18th Incident, the four northeastern provinces fell into enemy hands one after another. The three leagues and twenty-six banners in the eastern part of Inner Mongolia were also completely controlled by the Japanese military. The only remaining are the three leagues and twenty-three banners in the west. The territory is within the borders of the three provinces of Chahar, Suiyuan, and Ningxia. Although it is still under our country's jurisdiction, the Japanese military is watching covetously and has long regarded it as something in the bag. The Tanaka Memorial originally had the conspiracy to organize the "Mongolian Great Yuan Republic," with the intention of creating a second puppet regime. To the north, it would serve as a buffer to counter the forces of Soviet Russia in Outer Mongolia; to the south, it would serve as a base for invading the central provinces of our country.

In recent years, Japanese military personnel who have gone to various banners in Western Mongolia to contact and scout have been continuously on the road. Along the border between Rehe and Chahar, radio stations have been widely planted, roads have been built quickly, and troops and equipment have been accumulated, waiting for the time to move. Our country's border defense has been abandoned for years. The Japanese military can take advantage of it at any time and sweep through Western Mongolia. The reason why they are lingering between Guyuan and Duolun and not launching an attack is not because they have any concerns about us. It is only because Western Mongolia borders Outer Mongolia. Today, when their anti-Russian preparations have not yet been completed and their policy toward Russia has not yet been fully determined, they are unwilling to be too hasty. Therefore, after weighing the pros and cons and assessing the situation, the Japanese believe that the most appropriate strategy for Mongolia is to control the princes of Western Mongolia by means of intimidation and enticement, so that they will submit internally without a fight. In this way, it will neither cause major international resentment nor require them to assume responsibility for mobilizing troops. What plan could be better than this?

Although these Japanese strategies are revealed from time to time, they are difficult to conceal. Now, let's talk about those that are obvious and easy to see. For example, the military officer school was established in Wangye Temple in the Hinggan area a month or two ago, enrolling Mongolian youth and providing them with military education. It is planned to train tens of thousands of Mongolian troops in one or two years, providing them with food and equipment to become elite soldiers. Then, under the guise of revolution and independence, they will be used as pioneers for internal invasion. If a third party raises accusations and protests to them, they can claim that it is an internal dispute in Western Mongolia and has nothing to do with them. This is one aspect. A report from Rehe a few days ago stated that the fake organization demarcated the Ujimqin and Bairin banners of Inner Mongolia and placed them under the jurisdiction of the fake Hinggan Province. The princes of the two banners clashed with the Japanese and puppet troops in Linxi. The Bairin banner belongs to the Zhaomeng League in Rehe, which the Japanese have long regarded as their own. However, the Ujimqin banner belongs to the Ximeng League in Chahar Province and is not under the jurisdiction of the pseudo-Manchukuo. However, it has also been heard that it has been incorporated into the pseudo-province. Although the above news has not been confirmed, the future is long. Similar local annexation actions will eventually be difficult to guarantee that they have no intention. This is another aspect.

In the future, the Monglian Autonomous Government will be at the forefront of the facilities of inner mongolian autonomy, but the powers of the Military national defense are still in the hands of the central government. To this day, if our country still thinks of holding on to the overall situation in Inner Mongolia, it should rectify its troops and consolidate its border defenses so that the newly budding Inner Mongolian autonomy will not be destroyed. I sincerely hope that the central authorities and the leaders of the Monglian Autonomous Government's guiding officers will pay attention to this.

Hungarian Diplomatic Activities Pursue Contact with Italy and Poland Separately 20

Britain and Japan Are Both Active in Northern Europe 25

Soviet Russia Believes It Is Not a Coincidence

(Moscow) The Pravda newspaper commented on the visit of the British Lord Privy Seal Eden to the capitals of the Scandinavian countries, saying, "Mr. Eden's trip is to make Britain and the Scandinavian countries have closer political and economic ties. British imperialism is trying to strengthen its influence in these countries. Recently, Germany has also been particularly active there, so Papen's hasty trip to Stockholm after Aeton is by no means accidental. Britain's efforts to strengthen its influence in the Scandinavian countries are also directed at its allies and enemies, because Japan is also expanding its influence there. It is no secret that Japan has ordered munitions from Sweden. Swedish newspapers have also recorded it. In addition, the active activities of the Japanese intelligence department in Stockholm and Oslo, and the increasing frequency of Japanese officers visiting these countries, are all noteworthy. The Scandinavian countries are increasingly becoming a battlefield for political and economic conflicts among imperialists. (TASS, 20th)

Soviet Union Cracks Major Espionage Case 26

German Leader Specializes in Spying on Military Intelligence

Supreme Court Sentences to Eight Years Imprisonment

(Leningrad) The Military Tribunal of the Supreme Court of the Soviet Union is hearing a case of an espionage group. The group specializes in collecting secret information about the Soviet Army, Navy, military aircraft factories, and the defenses of Leningrad and Murmansk. The leader is a German named Fuchs, and the Austrian Kortegasse, an expert hired by Murmansk's Molnarobestroitorus, is Fuchs's closest assistant. Fuchs and Kortegasse communicated in cipher and used pseudonyms. The espionage organization also hired several Soviet people to work in Leningrad and Murmansk. The main person in Leningrad was Pozhikhovsky, who was ordered by Fuchs and Kortegasse to mark the location of the garrison and the large factories related to national defense, aviation bases, airfields, fuel depots, etc., on the Leningrad map. Gatlez, a Czechoslovak, was also entrusted by Fuchs to carry out the same work, marking the locations of power plants, gas plants, water plants, etc., that Leningrad would be attacked by air during wartime. However, Gatlez not only refused to comply, but also reported the matter to the National Political Department. Kortegasse recruited three employees of the Molnarobestroi plant in Murmansk to carry out espionage work. These three were Soviet citizens, Grinfeld, Petrovsky, and Gobchikov. They collected various secret information about the port's naval and commercial transportation. All the above-mentioned personnel were arrested in early August this year. All the reconnaissance materials were seized when Fuchs, Kortegasse, and Pozhikhovsky were arrested. The Supreme Court has sentenced Fuchs to eight years imprisonment, Kortegasse to six years imprisonment, and Soviet citizen Pozhikhovsky to death for betraying his country. Grinfeld, Petrovsky, and Gobchikov were each sentenced to ten years imprisonment. (TASS, 20th)

Naval Negotiation Points of Contention 27

Japan Will Demand Abolition of Aircraft Carriers

(London) Japan's demand to abolish aircraft carriers will be an important point of contention in the naval talks. It is reported that Representative Yamamoto has received instructions from the government to make every effort to demand the abolition of all existing aircraft carriers and prohibit their construction. Rear Admiral Isoroku Yamamoto previously served as commander of aircraft carriers, so he is very familiar with the effectiveness of this weapon. As for Japan's motive for demanding abolition, it is probably because this mobile air force base can be driven near the Japanese coast. A Japanese expert said, "We all know that aircraft carriers are useless for defense, but they are most fierce for attacking others. Fleets in the Pacific, without aircraft carriers, are not a threat to Japan." British and American officials, on the other hand, believe that Japan's countless islands are no different from aircraft carriers, because Japan will definitely be involved in wars in the Far East. The Japanese representative pointed out that this intention is a sign of deliberately invading Japan. At present, what Britain and the United States can agree to is probably only limiting the number and tonnage of aircraft carriers. Japan also advocates reducing battleships, but Britain and the United States regard battleships as the most valuable weapons. Therefore, no matter what the result, Japan's purpose is to retain a sufficient number of high-speed cruisers to control commerce in the Far East and be able to defend itself. It opposes other weapons that can attack, such as large battleships, aircraft carriers, and heavy cruisers. (National Telegram, 20th)

(Washington) As the London Naval Talks are about to be held, the Department of the Navy today issued a descriptive statement, specifically describing the naval policy of the United States, paying special attention to the types of warships. The Department of the Navy quoted the famous saying in football strategy, namely, "A strong offense is the only method of self-defense," expressing the Department's opposition to the drastic reduction of battleship tonnage, because battleships are the most powerful weapon for naval defense, "and the United States is separated from the future war stage by 7,500 miles." The so-called future war stage refers to the Far East. The Department of the Navy does not fully believe that naval air warfare will occupy the most important position as generally imagined, saying that the effectiveness of the air force has not been proven due to climate and other factors, so it cannot be fully trusted. The so-called theory that countless aircraft will destroy cities overseas is still an ideal talk. To achieve success with this type of attack, there must be a large-scale base near the attacked area. European countries are in a different position, because dozens of countries are gathered in one place, so they need a strong air force. The United States is not. The statement also stated that the air force is not as essential to the United States as it is to European countries. However, it also stated that the United States' naval aviation is superior to any country in the world in terms of both talent and material. The difference in opinion among Britain, the United States, and Japan regarding battleship tonnage is the most important issue in the current naval talks. It is recalled that the London talks in mid-July also encountered serious difficulties due to this. Britain advocated reducing the limitation of battleship tonnage from 35,000 tons to 25,000 tons, while the United States advocated maintaining the original tonnage. (National Telegram, 20th)

Japanese Airplanes and Airfields Use Cigarette Tin Foil as Funds 30

Gold Standard Group Signs Protocol 31

Maintain the Gold Content of Currencies of Various Countries

Increase Trade with Each Other by 10 Percent

(Brussels) Representatives of the world's remaining five gold standard countries signed a protocol here today, reaffirming their determination to maintain the current gold content of the currencies of the countries concerned. Representatives of the gold standard countries held meetings at the Belgian Ministry of Foreign Affairs for the past two days, chaired by Belgian Foreign Minister Jaspar. Today's meeting ended at 5:00 pm after the protocol was signed. The protocol stated that France, the Netherlands, Belgium, Italy, and Switzerland have decided to increase trade with each other by 10 percent for the sake of economic mutual assistance. Representatives of the countries had previously resolved to establish a permanent secretariat of the Gold Group in Brussels to handle various matters. (National Telegram, 20th)

(Brussels) The conference of the gold standard group of countries has just signed a protocol, which roughly states: "The representatives of the countries attending the meeting firmly believe that currency stability is necessary to restore the normal economic situation. Therefore, seeking the stability of the currencies of these countries is to seek the economic recovery of the world. This was stated by the representatives of the gold standard countries at the London Economic Conference in 1933. Now, in accordance with the desire to maintain the current gold parity, the following points are especially advocated: (1) A general committee shall be jointly organized by the representatives of the gold standard countries. (2) Regarding the exchange of goods between the gold standard countries, it is hoped that the actual trade volume will increase by 10 percent compared with the period from July 1, 1933, to June 30, 1934. As for the methods of increasing trade, they shall be negotiated bilaterally by the signatory countries. (3) Regarding tourism and transportation, it has been decided to organize two subcommittees to prepare reports on the proposals of the general committee or the proposals submitted to the general committee. The general committee will meet again in three months to accept this report and discuss future procedures." French Minister of Commerce Laimur, representing France, came here to participate in the conference of gold standard countries and recently declared that he was pleased with the preliminary results of the conference, saying that he was prepared to immediately conduct bilateral negotiations with Belgian Foreign Minister Jaspar to increase trade between the two countries. Negotiations with Italy will also begin soon. He also said that cooperation between the gold standard countries will not lead to a policy of restricting import quotas. (Havas, 20th)

In the 12,000-Mile Air Race Between England and Australia, Two English Aviators Take the Lead 33

Now Have Taken Flight to Singapore

Morrison Couple Thwarted in India

(Allahabad) In the England-Australia air race, Englishmen Scott and Black arrived here at 9:10 this morning. They stayed here for only one hour and ten minutes, and left for Singapore at 10:20, so they have now increased the distance ahead of others. (National Telegram, 21st)

(London) The Comet aircraft flown by English aviators Scott and Black is currently in the lead in the 12,000-mile London-Melbourne race. At 9:15 this morning, the aircraft had arrived in Allahabad. Scott told a Reuters interviewer that they had had a smooth journey since leaving Baghdad. They initially encountered head winds, but after entering India, they encountered tail winds. Except for avoiding the restricted area in the northwest province of India, they flew straight to Allahabad. Scott and others rested in Allahabad for one hour and took off again at 10:15, heading for Singapore.

The English aviator Morrison couple, who were originally flying the fastest, had an unfortunate encounter after leaving Baghdad. At 7:45 this morning, they were forced to land in Karachi, which is about 450 miles from Allahabad. They told a Reuters interviewer that they were afraid that the gasoline supply was insufficient to reach Allahabad directly, so they landed in Karachi. The night was foggy and they encountered head winds, but nothing else happened. At 11:15 in the morning, they took off again, but returned after only ten minutes because the machine was slightly damaged. A mechanic has been called to the Karachi airfield to carry out repairs, but they have not been completed by the afternoon. The Morrison couple decided to take off at 9:30 tonight, but were already two hours late.

The Dutch aircraft Douglas pilot Parmentier and Moll arrived in Baghdad at 11:11 and took off again at midnight, stopping briefly at Jask, a town on the Persian coast, and then took off again, arriving in Karachi at 8:50 in the morning. At 9:10, they proceeded to Allahabad.

The Dutch aircraft Pander pilot Asjes and Geyssendorfer arrived in Baghdad at 1:20 in the morning, took off again after 20 minutes, passed Karachi at 10:30, and went to Allahabad.

The American aviators Turner and Pangborn arrived in Baghdad at noon. They first circled in the sky for 15 minutes before descending. When landing, they came down quickly with the wind, which was different from others who came down against the wind. The fuselage was only a few inches away from the telephone pole. People in the airfield were speechless when they saw it. The ambulance attendant, expecting an accident, had already driven to rescue them. Although the American aviators finally survived unscathed, the spectators had been scared. After 40 minutes, Turner and Pangborn took off again. According to Turner, the weather in Europe was bad, and there was a lot of sand in the air when flying over Iraq, so the flight could not be fast.

The English aviators Jones and Waller arrived in Baghdad at 5:12 in the morning. When they departed from the Mildenhall airfield, they were carrying gasoline for 14 and a half hours of flight, and they were overdue. People in London and Baghdad were concerned about their safety, fearing that they had been forced to land in the desert. Now that they have safely arrived in Baghdad, they are relieved. It was observed that there was only one gallon of oil left in their machine. According to Waller, they flew from the Black Sea and, when passing through Persia, felt that there was very little gasoline, so they stopped the plane in a village to inspect it. They took off again this morning, causing a detour of 250 miles. This morning at 6:00, Jones and Waller took off, but returned shortly after because the machine was damaged and needed to be repaired. English Air Force officer Gillman, because the engine was damaged, dismantled the machine in Marseilles for inspection. The repairs were completed this morning and he flew to Rome at 9:10. (Reuters, 21st)

(Singapore) A Royal Air Force bomber, which was flying to Arohesiter for the London-Melbourne air race, is now missing. The authorities have dispatched several aircraft to find it. (Reuters, 21st)

(London) According to reports from various places, the London-Melbourne air race is progressing. The English aircraft are currently in a superior position. The aircraft flown by the Morrison couple is flying the fastest, followed by the aircraft flown by the Englishmen Scott and Black. The Dutch aircraft Douglas DC-2 is in third place. Mr. Morrison's aircraft averages more than 200 miles per hour, so it flew 2,553 miles in less than 13 hours after departure and arrived safely in Baghdad at 7:10 pm. The English community and Arab welcomers were extremely numerous. The Morrison couple rested for one hour and thirty minutes before taking off again and continuing forward. Mr. Morrison and others did not stop at all on one of the most difficult sections of the race, so no obstacles are likely to occur in the entire journey thereafter. Mr. Morrison told a Reuters reporter in Baghdad that their aircraft was flying high, hoping to avoid the bad weather at low altitudes. Although it was a long journey, it was extremely smooth. When they were about to arrive in Alipo, they were very anxious because the oil in the machine was running out, but they finally arrived safely in Baghdad, with only two hours of fuel remaining.

The aircraft flown by Scott and Black arrived in Baghdad 12 minutes after the Morrison couple took off. As for the Dutch aviators Parmentier and Moll, who were the first to arrive in Athens, they also made good progress. They arrived in Alipo at 7:47 last night and flew to Baghdad at 8:37. The aircraft they were flying was a Douglas DC-2. Parmentier told a Reuters interviewer in Athens that they had been flying at an average of about 190 miles per hour since leaving Mildenhall and were confident that they would be able to complete the entire journey safely.

In addition to these three aircraft making smooth progress, the remaining aircraft have suffered many misfortunes. Miss Cochrane, the only beautiful woman in the race, was the first to withdraw because she discovered that the engine in her machine was damaged after safely arriving in the Romanian capital last night. The aircraft flown by Air Force officer Gillman had its engine dismantled and inspected after arriving in Marseilles last night due to engine damage. However, Gillman hoped to continue today. In addition, there were two other aircraft that were delayed en route due to damaged parts. Also, the aircraft flown by Air Force Second Lieutenant Shaw was forced to land on the Spanish coast 40 miles northwest of Barcelona. He was waiting for permission from the authorities to set off again this morning.

Four aircraft passed through the second inspection station, Rome, at night. Two aircraft arrived in Athens last night, including the aircraft flown by the Americans Turner and Pangborn. According to Mr. Turner, their aircraft encountered headwinds all the way and passed through thick fog, so they did not stay in Rome and flew over Mont Blanc. The Comet aircraft flown by the Englishmen Scott and Black took off again at 9:33 in the evening and flew to Allahabad, 2,300 miles away.

The Dutch aircraft Douglas DC-2 flew to Baghdad at 11:11 in the morning and took off again at midnight. (Reuters, 21st)

(London) Colonel Fitzmaurice of Ireland withdrew from the England-Australia air race due to a dispute over the carrying capacity of his aircraft. He flew from the Mildenhall airfield to Croydon this afternoon. Mr. Fitzmaurice hopes to find an American aviation inspector to inspect his aircraft. If there is an obstacle, he will fly to Dublin to obtain the necessary certificates and then depart for Melbourne to compete with the official contestants. (Reuters, 21st)

(Batavia) The aircraft flown by Jones et al. in the England-Australia air race was forced to land on the Black Sea coast last night, surrounded by Persian villagers, and were hostile from time to time, so they had an uneasy night. They flew to this place this morning. When they were flying over the Black Sea, the weather turned bad and they used a lot of gasoline, so as soon as they reached the coast, they landed to refuel. The place they chose to land was in a field near a small Persian village. Not long after landing, they were surrounded by the local masses, who were very angry, so they stayed up all night guarding the aircraft. This morning, as soon as it dawned, they flew to this place. When they arrived here, there was only one gallon of gasoline left. Although they had this unpleasant experience last night, they still stated that they could continue flying after refueling. However, shortly after taking off, they turned back because the engine was slightly damaged. (National News Agency, 21st)

Japanese Personnel Rampant in Manchuria 35

(Khabarovsk) Deputy Director of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Mr. Melnikov, wrote to Director Li Shaogeng, stating that the actions of the railway police, guards, and officials from the Japanese military in forcefully occupying railway-owned buildings have become increasingly frequent recently. The letter specifies that they are not only occupying temporary empty houses but also the residences of railway staff and the buildings of railway agencies. The original responsibility of the police officers was to maintain law and order, the guards were established to protect the railway and employees, and the Japanese officers, according to their statements, came to maintain order, but they intend to enter the residences of railway staff, break locks, and forcibly evict railway staff, reversing the roles of guest and host. Such illegal actions have obviously disrupted the operations of the railway and its employees. Mr. Melnikov listed the illegal and violent actions of the Japanese and Manchurian authorities, and requested a swift resolution to vacate the occupied houses, cease illegal actions, and protect railway employees and their property, so that they are spared the violence of these self-proclaimed authorities. Yu Feipeng Expresses Gratitude to the Soviet Government 36

(Moscow) Chinese Vice Minister of Transportation, Yu Feipeng, upon leaving the Soviet Union for Europe, telegraphed the Soviet People's Commissar for Transportation, Mr. Lykov, from the border station of Negoreloye, saying, "I have had a very pleasant stay in your country. As I leave your border, I respectfully greet you. During our stay in your country, we received utmost care and hospitality, and we were honored to be shown the achievements of your great nation in detail. This gain is extremely beneficial to our country and is especially precious. For this, I and the members of my delegation dare to express our deep gratitude to you. Please convey this sentiment to your government and its representatives." (TASS Telegram, 20th)
