Osaka After the Wind and Flood Disaster (Japanese Correspondence) 70

Losses No Less Than 300 Million Yuan

Houses and Factories Mostly Recovered

Osaka, Japan, is especially familiar to us Chinese. For example, Japanese shipping companies, whether it is Nippon Yusen, Yamashita Kisen, Osaka Shosen, or Nisshin Kisen, are generally called Osaka companies, as if Osaka can represent Japan, or at least symbolize Japan. Indeed, Osaka is almost a representative of Japan, because more than 80% of its industrial manufactures, especially export commodities, exported to China, Southeast Asia, and other regions, are made in Osaka. Although this is not a port open to foreign trade, there are special ships regularly traveling to Tianjin, Shanghai, Hong Kong, Southeast Asia, and even Europe. However, the navigation of foreign ships can only be restricted to Kobe, and going to Osaka is restricted. However, the distance between Osaka and Kobe is originally very close. Recently, as a result of building factories and promoting foreign trade, these two places are about to become one.

Osaka has been completely formed into a modern city. In terms of population, it has more than 2.5 million people, and its area is probably larger than Shanghai, so it is not as crowded as Shanghai, but the air is worse than Shanghai. In the center of the Shanghai Public Concession, from Great Horse Road to Sixth Horse Road, and the Hongkou area, except for the Bund, it is not easy to see trees. In Osaka, from Osaka Station, south to the Yamato River, north to the Shin-Yodo River, except for Nakanoshima Park, it is also not easy to see a piece of green leaf. However, in Shanghai, you are dazed by the scent of powder and meat, while in Osaka, the smoke obscures the sky, making your nostrils black.

The means of transportation can indeed meet her industrial needs. The tram network is well organized, and it does not take much time to travel north and south. And it only costs six sen per day (about five cents in silver dollars) to travel throughout the city, which is really beneficial to the general public, workers, and students. In addition, the city-run buses are almost as developed as the trams, and the cost is also the same, because its purpose of operation is not to make money, but to seek the convenience of transportation and promote the development of its entire industry. The industry in Japan is not characterized by large industries, but by small factories competing for success. Even in such an industrial center as Osaka, there are still many small factories. Many large factories still subcontract parts to small factories, so cheap transportation tram, bus, etc. car fares have a greater effect.

In the past two or three years, the rural areas of Japan have been particularly difficult. The tax burden is very heavy, and the income from sideline businesses (such as silk income) has decreased, coupled with unprecedented natural disasters, so life is difficult. Most farmers are hungry. Cities especially Osaka, a city that occupies an absolute advantage in exports, are enjoying double favors and are of course extraordinarily prosperous. One is that heavy industry and quasi-heavy industry have benefited from military industry, and have made money invisibly and visibly. The second is that the Japanese government is making every effort to promote foreign development, use the falling yen exchange rate, and subsidize foreign export trade. Light industry has also received preferential treatment, but in reality, few people actually make money. Ordinary urban residents can only barely make ends meet, and the income of workers who rely on physical labor is relatively reduced due to the depreciation of the yen. Therefore, the general consumption power has not increased, and the good market situation is ultimately false.

Wind and flood disasters are particularly harmful in Osaka. Most of the factories in Taisho Ward and Port Ward were either flooded or blown down by the wind. How much the loss is, the official statistics are still not accurate now. The approximate estimate is no less than 300 million yuan. Together with the losses in Hyogo Prefecture and Kobe, the industrial sector has a total of 500 million yen. The Osaka shipping terminal is still irreparable, and it will take a considerable time to organize, and it will be more troublesome to recover. But one thing that is worthy of our surprise, and should also be noted, is that from the occurrence of the wind and flood disaster on the 21st of last month to now, only three weeks have passed. The ordinary places have naturally long been restored to order, and the traces of natural disasters are completely invisible. Even the ordinary houses in the "Bihana Ward", "Port Ward", "Taisho Ward" and other places with the most severe floods have gradually been repaired, leaving only some water stains. The repair of factories is easier for some, such as machinery factories, and more difficult for others, such as lumber mills and light industries, but they are working hard to resume operations as soon as possible. The Osaka municipal authorities have also hired engineers to guide the resumption of operations in small and medium-sized factories purely on a voluntary basis, and also provide them with the necessary working capital at low interest rates, so resumption of work is more convenient, but the recovery of losses is not easy, because the one-sided development of the city, like the stimulus of military demand industry, I am afraid it is difficult to last. (October 14, 1934, in Osaka)

Observations on Japanese and Soviet Military Affairs by a Certain Military Expert 71

The Soviet Union Can Triumph in Land, Air, and Chemical Warfare

Control of the Greater Khingan Range Will Determine Victory

(Harbin Dispatch) According to a certain military expert in Harbin familiar with the military preparations of Japan and the Soviet Union, the situation of the competition between Japan and the Soviet Union in the Far East has reached a point where the stakes are clear, and a large-scale war could break out at any time. Based on observations of the land, sea, and air forces of both sides, as well as the strategic and leadership capabilities of their military leaders, and the national finances, production capacity, and military resources, victory is likely to belong to the Soviet Union. A record of what the military expert said follows:

Japanese and Soviet Military Preparations (A) Land Forces: (1) Japanese Army: According to the budget for the tenth year proposed by the Japanese Ministry of the Army this August, the total amount is 680 million yuan. The peacetime strength is approximately 230,000 soldiers. The wartime strength is 25,000 soldiers per division, and the total number of mobilized personnel nationwide can increase to 5 million. (2) Soviet Army: The recent budget is unknown. According to a 1930 investigation by the International Disarmament Preparatory Commission, it was 778 million yuan. The regular army consists of 562,000 regular soldiers and 130,000 national security guards, totaling 692,000. According to a 1933 investigation, the Soviet regular army had increased to 1.3 million, and could increase to 7.5 million in wartime. (B) Naval Forces: (1) Japan: According to the Japanese Ministry of the Navy's budget for the tenth year, the total amount is 714.7 million yuan. The number of naval vessels includes 9 battleships, with a tonnage of 272,870; 4 aircraft carriers, with a tonnage of 68,870; 14 Class A cruisers, with a tonnage of 123,520; 20 Class B cruisers, with a tonnage of 93,375; 102 destroyers, with a tonnage of 121,056; 71 submarines, with a tonnage of 77,842, totaling 220 vessels, with a tonnage of 756,242. The above statistics are based on a survey conducted on February 31, 1933. (2) Soviet Union: 4 battleships, with a tonnage of 23,370; 4 cruisers, 5 ironclad ships, 23 destroyers, 6 torpedo boats, 15 submarines, 25 motorboats, 2 gunboats, 20 minesweepers, 7 river gunboats, 1 seaplane carrier, totaling 112 vessels. The above is based on 1931 statistics, many of which are old ships with very weak combat capabilities. According to recent news, the Soviet Union has deployed many warships in Vladivostok, including 15 submarines and 60 small torpedoes. Most of these torpedoes are the latest weapons invented by France, equipped with four torpedo launch tubes and four heavy machine guns, with a maximum speed of 40 to 50 knots. (C) Air Forces: (1) Japanese Air Force: According to a survey conducted four years ago, the number of Japanese aircraft was 850 for the army and 460 for the navy. According to a recent survey, the types and numbers of aircraft include 11 reconnaissance squadrons, 11 fighter squadrons, 49 bomber squadrons, and 3 training schools, totaling 26 squadrons. (2) Soviet Air Force: Since the completion of the Soviet Five-Year Plan, its ideal of an invincible air force has been realized. According to "The Threat of the Red Russian Air Force" by Takashi Noguchi, the Soviet Air Force has 20 air brigades in the army, each brigade consisting of an air bomber team of 50 bombers and an air fighter team of 60 fighters, with a total of 2,200 aircraft. There are 48 large detachments and 60 independent squadrons deployed throughout the country. Each squadron has 2 platoons, each platoon consisting of 3 aircraft. Independent squadrons consist of 8 aircraft. In addition, there are 10 balloon teams and 3 airships. In the navy, there are 2 bomber detachments, 6 independent bomber squadrons, fighter squadrons, reconnaissance squadrons, and the Far Eastern Fleet's seaplane aviation team, totaling 220 teams. The distribution is as follows: 78 reconnaissance squadrons, 68 fighter squadrons, 49 bomber squadrons, 6 training squadrons, and 24 naval aircraft teams, currently deployed in the Far East (east of the Urals), under the jurisdiction of the Novosibirsk Military Region, including one bomber squadron in Amursk, one bomber detachment in Irkutsk, one seaplane aviation team in Boli, one reconnaissance squadron in Chita, two bomber squadrons in Novosibirsk, one reconnaissance squadron in Spassk, and one reconnaissance squadron in Vladivostok. According to the above descriptions of the sea, land, and air forces of Japan and the Soviet Union, the Soviet navy is clearly inferior to Japan. However, in terms of land forces, Japan is far inferior to the Soviet Union. In addition, Japan is also unlikely to have an advantage in mechanical equipment suitable for both peacetime and wartime. A comparison is as follows: armored trains: Soviet Union 38 teams plus one brigade, Japan unknown; armored vehicles: Soviet Union 15 teams, Japan unknown; tank teams: Soviet Union 3 regiments, Japan 1 squadron; telegraph teams: Soviet Union 12 regiments, Japan 2 regiments.

Strategic Observations Furthermore, strategically speaking, Japan also has many disadvantages. According to the military expert, if Japan goes to war with the Soviet Union, there are three strategic threats it would face: (1) the Soviet Union's concentrated attack strategy; (2) the plain warfare in Hulunbuir; and (3) the Soviet Union's chemical warfare. The concentrated attack strategy is advocated by General Galen, commander of the Far Eastern Military District, and many other military leaders, such as Air Force Staff Officer Chad. This strategy is implemented when the fighting between the two armies is most intense. In a combat emergency, artillery engages in fierce artillery battles with the enemy in fixed positions, while fighter planes provide cover for the battlefield, attack aircraft raid the enemy's mobile units, bombers attack the enemy's air force bases, and several tanks charge into the enemy's positions. Then, the air force advances with a large group of hundreds of aircraft at full strength, annihilating the enemy in one fell swoop. This is the so-called concentrated attack strategy. The plain warfare in the Hulunbuir region is good for using the above strategy to subdue Japan. What Japan fears most about plain warfare is not the large number of Soviet troops, but the threat of the Soviet air force. Therefore, Japanese military experts advocate that if Japan is not confident in plain warfare, it should retreat to the Greater Khingan Range and use small forces to advance and retreat in the Hulunbuir area to contain the Soviet army's advance. The Soviet Union's chemical warfare is also something that puts the Japanese military in a difficult position. It is said that each Soviet division has a gas officer, and all divisions and flight units have a chemical warfare platoon. There are also special military training teams for gas officers and military chemists. Gas masks have been distributed to all soldiers and horses. In terms of industrial mobilization, military resources, and national finances, Japan is also unlikely to have an advantage. The Soviet Union is a socialist country, and all domestic industries are state-owned, so it can be said that the entire country is mobilized. The success of the Five-Year Plan has made finances no longer a problem. The completion of the Siberian double-track railway has removed obstacles to military resources. On the other hand, Japan is facing a deficit in finances due to the expansion of its navy, army, and air force, coupled with domestic economic panic, which makes its finances even more difficult. In other aspects, such as the leadership of military leaders and the guidance of affiliated allies, the two countries are evenly matched. Japan can use the puppet state, while the Soviet Union can contact the United States and China. Although Japanese military leaders are strong, the Soviet army's party members are also quite strong. It is said that in 1928, they accounted for 22.6%, and by 1933, they had increased to 59.4%. Although Japan is inferior to the Soviet Union in many ways, it also has advantages over the Soviet Union. First, Japan has completed the railway network in Northeast China. Second, Japan's military resources do not need to be obtained from afar, but can be directly obtained from Northeast China or North China. Third, the powerful Japanese navy can threaten the Soviet fortress of Vladivostok.

Final Victory According to the above, the two armies each have their strengths and weaknesses. So, to whom will victory belong, and where will the outcome be determined? According to "The Red Army's Far Eastern Operations" by Japanese military expert Susumu Hirata, "The struggle between Japan and Russia will take place mainly in the Greater Khingan Range. This is recognized by military experts in both countries." Therefore, the mission of the troops stationed in Chita is to seize the Greater Khingan Range with lightning speed. If the Soviet army occupies this mountain range and builds solid fortifications to attack the Eastern Provinces, the Japanese army will be in a difficult situation because the Japanese army must attack uphill against the Soviet army and suffer great sacrifices. Moreover, the Greater Khingan Range is full of pines and cypresses, which are lush and towering, so all kinds of positional warfare and mountain warfare are ready. The difficulties and hardships can be imagined. Conversely, if the Japanese army occupies the area first, the Soviet army will also suffer the same pain. Therefore, if the Japanese army based in Qiqihar and the Soviet army based in Manzhouli launch an attack at the same time, one reaching the east side of the mountain range and the other reaching the west side of the mountain range, the two armies will inevitably engage in a fierce battle for the mountain. Whoever can seize the summit can win the final victory of the war. However, the Soviet Union also has chemical warfare, which Japan is no match for. The poisonous gas used by the Soviet army is an orange mist that can remain for a week. Soldiers must wear protective clothing at all times, and the vegetation in the poisoned area will wither. Its intensity can be imagined. On the other hand, the Soviet Union has a strong air force and a strong land force, as well as concentrated attack and Hulunbuir plain warfare, which are enough to put the Japanese army in a difficult situation. Therefore, as a result, if a war breaks out between Japan and the Soviet Union, the Soviet Union has the possibility of achieving the final victory. However, it must be stated that this is a judgment based on the current material foundation of Japan and the Soviet Union. As for the participation of other countries or other events, it is difficult to predict who will ultimately win.

Japanese and Puppet Troops Suddenly Arrived Outside Gubeikou 72

Demanding to Enter the War Zone to Suppress Bandits

Sternly Rejected by Huo Shi

Tianjin Correspondence, On the morning of the 17th of this month, more than 600 Japanese and puppet troops, including infantry, cavalry, and artillery, suddenly arrived outside Gubeikou. Among them was a Japanese captain as the company commander. He met with Huo Shi, the director of the Gubeikou Office of the Jizhou-Miyun Administrative Commissioner's Office, requesting permission for the Japanese and puppet troops to pass through Gubeikou and Caojialu in order to go to the war zone bordering Jixian, Yutian, and Zunhua to suppress bandits. The captain also said that bandits had recently sprung up in the war zone, and Japanese and Korean residents felt insecure. The Chinese security forces were unable to pacify the area, so they came to assist in the suppression. Huo Shi immediately refused, telling him that although bandits had been found in the war zone, they were all small groups, and the Hebei Provincial Security Forces were strong enough to suppress them. There was no need for foreign troops to enter to assist in the suppression, so as to avoid causing panic among merchants and residents and causing misunderstandings. The Japanese captain insisted on entering, and the troops remained outside Gubeikou. Huo Shi telegraphed Yin Rugeng for instructions. Yin, who had been inspecting Malanyu, was on his way back, passing through Yutian, and accompanied by Japanese military attache Shibayama, to investigate the Miyakoshi incident. He had not yet received a report on this matter.

Miyakoshi Incident: After Yin Rugeng and Shibayama investigated this time, Yin will report to the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, and another negotiation will resolve the matter. Yutian County Chief Chen Baosheng was deemed by the authorities to have failed to adequately protect foreigners in advance and failed to work hard afterward. Therefore, he has been replaced, and Huang Zhongkai has been appointed to fill the vacancy. He went to take over on the 16th of this month. Huang is a graduate of Meiji University in Tokyo, Japan, and has served as a secretary in the Pingjin military and political councils. In the future, diplomatic relations with Japan may be more effective. As for the bandits in the war zone, Zunhua, Yutian, Jixian, Fengrun, Huairou, and Miyun are still the most numerous. Large groups are stationed near the Great Wall line, confronting the local militias in the interior, while small groups are scattered everywhere, seizing opportunities to loot when the militia's suppression efforts are insufficient. On the 15th of this month, more than 100 bandits rushed in from the Yanshan Pass area, looting villages along the way and seizing a lot of weapons. No small number of hooligans were willing to join the bandits. Therefore, in just one day, the number of bandits had expanded to 170 or 180, and many men and women were kidnapped as hostages. The Zunhua militia and the war zone security forces were informed and jointly suppressed the bandits. A fierce battle broke out near Malanyu for two hours. The bandits were overwhelmed and abandoned several hostages. The rest of the bandits fled toward the pseudo-Jehol border. The puppet troops stationed in Malanyu Qingling, fearing that the bandits would return to the interior of Jehol, sent two companies of soldiers to intercept them. The bandits desperately resisted. After two hours of fighting, the puppet troops killed more than a dozen people, and the interception was slightly loosened. The bandits fled toward Zhongyingzi. In the northern mountains of Xinglong County, near the Dashui and Xiaodaoshui mining areas, there is also a group of bandits, numbering around 300, with guns and machine guns. They are hiding and have not come out, probably planning to take the opportunity to harass northern Zunhua. Therefore, the militias are heavily armed. (18th)

Luo Binghui's Band Fleed from Anhui to Jiangxi and Suffered a Major Defeat 73

丨Surrounded and Expected to Be Annihilated丨

Nanchang Correspondence, The pseudo-Seventh Army Corps of bandit Luo Binghui has been defeated everywhere from Fujian to Zhejiang to Anhui, and its elite troops have been almost wiped out. When the bandits recently fled to the Liukou area of Qimen, the Jiangxi border troops rushed to encircle and suppress them, and achieved considerable gains. Luo Binghui, in desperation, led the remaining 2,000 to 3,000 people to the area bordering Fuliang, Qimen, and Qiupu. Chen Tiaoyuan also ordered Li Zongjian's troops to suppress them. On the 13th of this month, a fierce battle broke out with the pseudo-Ninth Army Corps near Yaqiao in northern Fuliang, near the Anhui border. According to a telegram from Li's brigade to the headquarters on the 15th, in this battle, more than 200 people, including Peng Hanwei, commander of the Third Division of the pseudo-Seventh Army Corps, and Shi Qinan, commander of the pseudo-regiment, were killed, more than 40 bandits were captured, and 60 rifles, several light and heavy machine guns, and 3 telescopes were seized. Luo Binghui has now been surrounded by the Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui armies, and is expected to be annihilated.

Taiwan's Population Soars 74

An Increase of 122,843 People Last Year

Four Times the Birth Rate of Japan

Xiamen Correspondence, Taiwan, a small island located on the boundary between the tropical and temperate zones of the Pacific Ocean, has a mild climate and comfortable living conditions, resulting in a continuous increase in population fertility. The soaring birth rate in Taiwan is considered the highest in the world. The population dynamics statistics for Taiwan in 1933, published by the Taiwan Governor-General's Office at the end of September, are sufficient to reveal the true picture of Taiwan's population boom (the following statistics exclude the indigenous Taiwanese tribes, because the so-called Taiwanese today are descendants of people from southern Fujian who migrated to Taiwan and constitute the basic population of Taiwan).

The total population surveyed in 1933 was 4,974,157. The statistics are divided into six categories: marriage, divorce, birth, stillbirth, mortality, and increase.

(1) Marriage: The total number of marriages was 44,078, an average of 121 per day. The ratio per thousand people is about 9 (8.9). Compared with the previous year (1932), there was an actual increase of 955 cases, but the ratio per thousand people was approximately the same. By race, Taiwanese accounted for 43,001 cases, Japanese 900 cases, and foreigners 176 cases (mostly Chinese overseas). There was only one Korean case. Also, by race, the ratio per thousand people was 9.2 for Taiwanese, 4 for foreigners, 3.5 for Japanese, and 0.8 for Koreans (Note: the total number of marriages in Japan in 1933 was 515,270, with a ratio of 7.8 per thousand people).

(2) Divorce: The total number of divorces was 3,949, an average of 11 per day, a decrease of 36 compared to the previous year. The divorce rate per hundred marriages in 1933 was 9, and in 1932 it was 9.2, a decrease compared to the previous year. The ratio per population was 0.8 in both years. Analysing the number of divorces by race, apart from 11 Japanese cases and 4 foreign cases, the remaining 3,934 cases were all Taiwanese. Also, by race, the divorce rate per thousand people was 0.8 for Taiwanese, and very low for Japanese and others (Note: the total number of divorces in Japan in 1933 was 51,437, with a ratio of 0.8 per thousand people, and a marriage-divorce ratio of 10).

(3) Birth: The total number of births was 221,350, an average of 606 per day, 25 per hour, or one birth every two minutes and twenty-four seconds. This is far from the Japanese statistic of four births per minute (one birth every 15 seconds) in 1933. However, in terms of the ratio per thousand people, Taiwan has 44.5, while Japan has 31.6. Therefore, the birth rate in Taiwan is much higher than in Japan. Analysing the total number of births by race, Taiwanese accounted for 211,737, Japanese 7,979, foreigners 1,613, and Koreans 21. By the ratio per thousand people, Taiwanese accounted for 45.4, foreigners 36.8, Japanese 31.1, and Koreans 17.6. The total number of births actually increased by 7,158 compared to the previous year, and there was an increase of 0.3 per thousand people compared to the previous year (Note: the total number of births in Japan in the same year was 2,121,125).

(4) Stillbirth: The total number of stillbirths (i.e., miscarriages) was 7,885, an average of 22 stillbirths per day, with a ratio of about 1.5 per thousand people, an actual increase compared to the previous year. By race, Taiwanese accounted for 7,417, with a ratio of 1.6, Japanese 389, with a ratio of 1.5, foreigners 77, with a ratio of 1.8, and Koreans 2, with a ratio of 1.7 (Note: the total number of stillbirths in Japan in the same year was 119,579, with a ratio of 1.8).

(5) Mortality: The total number of deaths was 98,507, an average of 270 per day, or one death every five minutes and twenty-seven seconds. This is dozens of times different from the Japanese statistic of 2.3 deaths per minute in the same year. Analysing the number of deaths by race, Taiwanese accounted for 94,975, Japanese 2,747, foreigners 774, and Koreans only 11. By the ratio per thousand people, 20.3 Taiwanese died per thousand people, 17.7 foreigners, 10.7 Japanese, and 9.2 Koreans. Comparing the mortality rate per thousand people in Taiwan and Japan, Taiwan was 19.8 and Japan was 17.8. Comparing the mortality rate per thousand people in Taiwan in 1933 and 1932, there was a decrease of 0.7 (Note: the total number of deaths in Japan in 1933 was 1,193,916). (6) State of Increase: Overall, the population of Taiwan increased by 122,843 in the past year, with births subtracting deaths, an average increase of 337 per day, and an increase of about 24.7 per thousand people. Compared with 1932, there was an increase of one per thousand people. By race, Taiwanese increased by 25 per thousand people, which is the most alarming number, followed by Japanese with an increase of 20.4, then foreigners (mostly Chinese overseas) with an increase of 19.2, and Koreans also had an increase of 8.4. Comparing the natural increase rate of 13.8 per thousand people in Japan in the same year with 24.7 in Taiwan, the population increase rate in Taiwan is almost double that of Japan.

Page 9

Northwest Inspection Notes Special Reporter Keng Ya

Special Products of Gansu Province and Scenic Spots of Lanzhou City 75

Gansu Province has a vast territory and abundant treasures. The special products are particularly numerous and diverse. The most famous are: (1) Yak: Produced in Min County, Lintan, Yongdeng, and other counties. Local villagers hunt and eat them. The tail can be made into a tassel and sold in Beijing, Tianjin, and other places, generating substantial profits each year. (2) White Lamb: Produced in Gaolan, Jingyuan, Hongshui, and other places. The lambskin is light and warm and can be made into leather clothing. Every summer and autumn, it is transported by yellow sand skin rafts to Ningxia, Baotou, and other areas for sale, which is a major source of income for Gaolan and other regions. (3) Black Lamb: Produced in Lintan. Its skin can be made into clothing and is more durable than white lambskin. It is more expensive and sold in Tianjin, Shanghai, and other places. (4) Mountain Goat: Found in all major forests of Gansu Province. They are very fierce. Their blood can be used for medicine, and the meat is fishy. It can also be used to make fake musk. (5) Antelope: Produced in the northern mountains of Gaolan. Antelope horn is a valuable medicinal material. (6) Musk Deer: Produced in Pingliang, Qingyang, Wuwei, Longnan, and other places. Musk deer brains are musk, which is a top-grade medicine. It has a fast and effective cure for diseases and is also very expensive. Its skin has the distinction of "Tianma," "Wuyun Leopard," and "Auspicious Leopard," which are extremely light and warm when used for leather clothing. (8) Golden Monkey: Produced in Wen County. (9) Leopard: Produced in Lintan, Min County, Heshui, and other places. The skin is divided into two types: "golden coin" and "artemisia leaf." The skin has the widest range of uses. (10) Lynx: Produced in Lintan, Min County, Yumen, and Dunhuang. It is divided into three types: "sheep lynx," "horse lynx," and "grass lynx." Its skin can also be used for leather jackets, but it is expensive. It is sold in Beijing, Tianjin, Shanghai, Wuhan, and other places every year. (7) Sand Fox: Produced in Yongdeng. (11) Bear: Produced in Wen County. Those with golden hair are the best, and the paws are the best medicine. (12) Deer: Most numerous in various counties of Longnan. Their antlers can be used as medicine and are sold both inside and outside the province every year, making it a major source of income for Longnan. (13) Horse Chicken: Produced in Lintan. Its tail can be used as shuttle threads, and it is sold both domestically and abroad every year. (14) Honey Bees: Most numerous in Pingliang, Jingchuan, Qingyang, Guyuan, Wudu, Tianshui, and other places. The honey is divided into two types: red and white. White honey is the sweetest. (15) Cordyceps Sinensis: Produced in Wen County. It is a good medicine. (16) Calculus Bovis: Produced in Lintan. It is also a very important medicine. A significant quantity is sold in various provinces every year. (17) Pigeon Fish: Produced in the estuary of Jingyuan River. It is caught by chiseling ice in winter. It resembles a pigeon in shape, hence the name. It is popularly said to be transformed from true pigeons throwing themselves into the water, which is a far-fetched theory. However, it tastes very good. Local people often use it to treat guests, which has a unique flavor. (18) Nahai Beans: Produced in Zhangye. They resemble cherries in shape and are red and white in color with a fragrant taste. (19) Drunken Melon: Produced in Gaolan. It tastes sweet and has a slight alcoholic aroma, hence the name. It is also called cantaloupe, which is said to have originated from Hami. (20) Bracken: Produced in Gaolan, Longxi, Pingliang, and Qingyang. The roots can be pounded into powder, and the stems can be used to make soup and dishes. (21) Leek: Produced in Gaolan. The flower stalk is fat and tastes sweet, ranking first in the entire province. (22) Soft Pear: Produced in Gaolan. In severe winter, the skin is black, and the flesh is soft. It can relieve coal poisoning and tastes extremely sweet. (23) Tobacco: The tobacco produced in Hongniguo, Gaolan, is the most beautiful. In addition, Lintao, Yuzhong, and Taosha also have it, but it is inferior to Gaolan tobacco. It is sold in various southeastern provinces every year, which is the largest source of income for each of these counties.

According to the Chamber of Commerce's investigation, the annual import and export volume of Gansu Province is as follows: The exports are: (1) Gaolan, Yuzhong, Lintao, Jingyuan, and other counties produce 35,000 dan of self-made cotton water tobacco, with a value of 100 yuan per dan, totaling 3.5 million yuan. It is sold in Tianjin, Shanghai, Sichuan, Xinjiang, and other places. (2) Lintan, Min County, and other counties produce 3,400 dan of rhubarb and angelica, with a value of 240 yuan per dan, totaling 816,000 yuan. It is sold in Tianjin, Shanghai, and other places. (3) Yongchang, Haiyuan, Xiahe, and other counties produce 8,000 dan of sheepskin, including about 3,000 dan of "second hair" and about 5,000 dan of old sheepskin, with a value of 800 yuan per dan for "second hair" and 120 yuan per dan for old sheepskin, totaling 3 million yuan. It is sold in Pingjin, Shanghai, Wuhan, and other ports. (4) Wool: It is not organized into bales, so it is difficult to determine the exact amount. However, about 4 million jin of Qinghai wool passes through Gansu and is transported to Tianjin and Suiyuan, with a value of 20 yuan per 100 jin, totaling 800,000 yuan. The total value of the above-mentioned exports from Gansu Province each year is 7,316,000 yuan, plus the wool passing through Qinghai, the total value is 8,116,000 yuan.

The imports are: (1) About 6,000 bolts of wool and linen fabrics are transported from Tianjin and Shanghai, of which 4,000 bolts are wool fabrics and 2,000 bolts are linen fabrics. Wool fabrics are worth 140 yuan per bolt, and linen fabrics are worth 12 yuan per bolt, totaling 560,000 yuan. (2) About 500 bolts of silk and satin are transported from Suzhou, Hangzhou, Sichuan, and other places, of which 200 bolts are silk and 300 bolts are satin. Silk is worth 30 yuan per bolt, and satin is worth 50 yuan per bolt, totaling 21,000 yuan. (3) 4,600 bolts of various cotton fabrics are transported from Tianjin, Shanghai, Shanxi, and other places, with a price of 13 yuan per bolt, totaling 59,800 yuan. (4) 2,500 rolls of coarse cloth are transported from Hebei, Hubei, Shaanxi, and other places, with a price of 80 yuan per roll, totaling 200,000 yuan. (5) 1,000 dan of cotton are transported from Shaanxi and Xinjiang, with a price of 80 yuan per dan, totaling 80,000 yuan. (6) The Qinghai army imports 10,000 shi of wheat and miscellaneous grains, of which wheat accounts for 6,000 shi and miscellaneous grains account for 4,000 shi. Wheat weighs 1,200 jin per shi and is valued at 65 yuan. Miscellaneous grains weigh 1,100 jin per shi and are valued at 50 yuan, totaling 590,000 yuan. (7) 550 dan of paper cigarettes are transported from Tianjin and Shanghai, which are divided into three types: "Three Gun," "Hartmann," and "Beauty," with a price of 500 yuan per dan, totaling 275,000 yuan. (8) Hunan official tea is transported through the territory for sale to Qinghai and Xinjiang, 230 tickets, with a value of 1,700 yuan per ticket, totaling 391,000 yuan. The total value of the above-mentioned imports into Gansu Province each year is 1,785,800 yuan, plus the official tea passing through Hunan, the total value is 2,176,800 yuan.

Forests: Gansu Province has a vast territory and sparse population, with mountains and valleys crisscrossing. During the Ming and Qing dynasties, there were many forests in various places. Since the Republic of China, there has been a lack of advocacy, and protection has been inadequate. As a result, most of the natural forests have been chopped down by the local people, resulting in the so-called "poor mountains and hungry waters." In recent years, although the construction of [illegible text] has shocked the national afforestation movement, attention has gradually been paid to it, and planting has been advocated repeatedly. However, due to the difficulty of funding in the past and the changes in the political situation, the so-called afforestation movement has become a mere formality. If the counties are not strictly ordered to protect the existing forests and actively increase the planting of new forests in a down-to-earth manner in the future, the future crisis will not only be a lack of timber, but also the already dry climate will be even more intense.

Mineral Products: The reserves are abundant, and they have been thoroughly investigated and intermittently mined by people. (1) Gold mines: The producing areas are Dunhuang, Jiuquan, Anxi, Yongdeng, Gaolan, Pingliang, Tianshui, Qingshui, Zhuanglang, Dongle, Jingyuan, Lintao, Xigu, Cheng County, etc. (2) Silver mines: The producing areas are Shandan, Yongdeng, Ningding, Lintao, Gaolan, Wen County, Cheng County, Liangdang, etc. (3) Mercury: The producing areas are Wen County, Wudu, etc. (4) Oil: The producing areas are Yumen, Jiuquan, Dunhuang, etc. (5) Coal mines: Distributed everywhere, almost throughout the province. Residents dig only a few zhang into the ground to find coal, but they are dug and abandoned, which is a pity. (6) Salt mines: Produced in Dunhuang, Gaotai, Minqin, Hongshui, Yongdeng, Jingyuan, Xihe, and other counties. (7) Copper mines: Produced in Gaolan, Taosha, Lintan, Hongshui, Yumen, and other counties. (8) Iron mines: Produced in Yongdeng, Gulang, Huining, Cheng County, Liangdang, Min County, Lintan, and other counties. (9) Lead mines: Produced in Yongdeng, Wuwei, Jingyuan, Min County, Cheng County, etc. (10) Asbestos: Produced in Wuwei, Yongchang, Huating, Tianshui, and other counties. In addition, Gaolan, Yongdeng, and other counties also produce manganese ore, and Gaotai, Yongdeng, Gaolan, Huating, and other counties also produce pottery clay. In short, Gansu Province has these treasures, especially gold and silver mines, which are like cash in hand. In the midst of the high calls for developing the Northwest, we must not allow the treasures to be abandoned on the ground for a long time.

Lanzhou is located south of Gaolan and controls the Yellow River to the north. From a distance, it is surrounded by mountains and water, with a tight and strict image. From a closer look, the high passes and rapids have a magnificent momentum. The climate is mild, and there are many beautiful forests and springs. Yesterday, thanks to my friends Guo Shifen and Du Yutian, I toured the Five Springs Mountain, Xiaoxihu, Beita, Jinshan Temple, Zhuangyan Temple, etc. The pavilions and clouds, the pines and cypresses are intertwined, and everywhere it shows that Lanzhou City is not only an important town in the western border, but also a famous scenic spot in the northwest. However, in the fifth month of the lunar calendar, during the so-called "City God's Birthday," various charity organizations compete to chant scriptures and offer dramas, lasting for more than ten days. The thousand candles in the main hall are constantly burning, and the Kangxi Sacred Edict of the former Qing Dynasty is still recited, which is too superstitious. "The city loves high buns, four feet high," the city is so supportive of the city's prosperity, and the countryside is even more afraid of little ghosts.

Overlooking the Yellow River from the north city, I often see fishermen catching fish along the shore, first catching them with small nets and then raising them in large nets in the river. Some so-called philanthropists go to buy them. Ordinary nets contain more than a hundred fish, and the price is always more than 20 yuan. The business seen on that day was that two nets were priced at 56 yuan in total. It is said that there are more small fish than large fish, which means that more lives are waiting to be saved. The philanthropist muttered scriptures, untied the net with his own hands, and released the fish into the river, called "releasing life." However, the fishermen downstream were already waiting to catch them. Looking back at the surrounding crowd, most of them were poor farmers who had fled from the countryside, without food and clothing. The danger to their lives is no different from the fish in the net. I remember that if philanthropists could transfer the money they used to release fish to run a factory for the poor or to subsidize the rural areas, then in terms of Buddhism, "saving a life is like building a seven-story pagoda," which would not only benefit the society alone. It is also heard that the local people of Lanzhou are not good at eating fish, and most of those who eat fish are foreigners. Therefore, although Lanzhou is adjacent to the Yellow River, a natural fish pond, it is impossible to find a fish market in the city.

The financial institutions in Lanzhou currently include (1) the Lanzhou branch of the Central Bank, which only operates domestic remittances; (2) the Gansu Ping City Official Money Bureau, which operates deposits and withdrawals and remittances. The Department of Finance plans to expand it and change it to the Gansu Farmers Bank; (3) Money houses and silver houses, which have a wider range of businesses than banks, followed by auxiliary financial institutions that are inadequate, and the pawnshop industry, which has a direct relationship with ordinary people. Large pawnshops charge a monthly interest of 3%, with a redemption period of three years, which is unsustainable and has gone bankrupt. Small pawnshops have no fixed interest rate, and the longest term is three months, which has been banned. Medium pawnshops charge a monthly interest of 5%, with a redemption period of one year. It is heard that the Department of Finance is planning to find a way to reduce interest rates and extend the period for the pawnshop industry. The ordinary loan interest rate is about 2-3%. Currency: (1) Current silver dollars, that is, Yuan Datou and Sun Yat-sen silver coins, copper auxiliary coins are ten or twenty copper coins. (2) Paper money: various banknotes of the Central Bank, four types of copper coin notes issued by the Official Money Bureau: ten, twenty, fifty, and one hundred, are all in common use. Ordinary silver coins of one yuan can be exchanged for 600 copper coins, that is, 6,000 wen. If you exchange for copper coin notes, you can only get 4,000 wen, that is, the price of copper coin notes on the market is one-third higher than the price of copper coins. Paper money from other counties is rarely circulated.

Dangerous Engineering Occurs in the Lower Reaches of the Yellow River in Shandong 76

Wang Wangzhuang and Dama Jia are being rescued

The water level in Shaanxi Prefecture has dropped, but it is still rising in Shandong

Jinan Correspondence, the water level of the Yellow River this year is very high. Although the Changyuan River Dam in southern Hebei has collapsed, no danger has occurred in this province so far. The River Affairs Bureau has issued an order to the entire river on the 18th to withdraw the defenses, and all defending and defending committee members and inspectors have been transferred back to Jinan. In another four or five days, the Frost's Descent period will arrive, and Anlan can be reported. Unexpectedly, due to the poor discharge of the tail, the water level of the entire river has receded slowly, the flood period is long, and the scouring is too severe. Today, dangerous works suddenly occurred in Dama Jia in the territory of Lijin County on the north bank of the lower reaches and Wang Wangzhuang in the territory of Patai County. Officials, soldiers, and civilians are currently rushing to protect them. According to the telegram from Duan Chang Zhou Yumei, many stone protections along Wang Wangzhuang have been washed away, and the first rake is dormant. After receiving the report, the River Affairs Bureau believed that the material affairs of the section were complete, and it was easy to rush to the rescue, but the newly purchased straw materials had not yet been inspected and accepted. It specifically telegraphed back to Zhou Yumei to pay attention to supervising the work and rushing to protect, and to allow the use of straw materials when necessary. There are also dangerous works between the ladder dam of Zhao Jia Ba in the lower reaches, and the straw materials in the lower section of Tang Jia Sao Jia Sao Dam are rotten. Due to the large water flow and the fierce flow, the situation is unstable, and it will need to be replaced in the future. In addition, each section in this province reported rising water levels today, and the water level at Luokou was 30 meters, 2 inches, and 4 inches, which is an unprecedented phenomenon. Yesterday, the water level in Shaanxi Prefecture, Henan was 293 meters and 5 inches, and the flow rate was 5,250 cubic meters. This morning, the water level was 292 meters and 9 inches 7, which was 5 inches 3 lower than the scissors. Today, the flow rate has also been reduced to 3,250 cubic meters. However, a telegram came this afternoon that the water level had receded to 292 meters and 5 inches 8, and the flow rate had also been reduced to 2,950 cubic meters. According to the usual practice, although the water level is low in autumn, the strength is submerged, and accidents occur every time, so it is not optimistic. Zhang Lianjia, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, went to Luokou in the north of Jinan City today to inspect and re-defend the river.

The Yellow River Conservancy Commission is currently conducting a detailed survey of the entire river and planning for overall remediation. The first survey team has already departed. Engineer Mu Zhifang is the leader of the team and is surveying between Lanfeng and Kaocheng. Because there is a section of the dam where the junction of Hebei and Henan is not connected, although there are people, the embankment is also very low and thin, which is very worrying. Therefore, great attention is paid to this place. The second survey team is preparing to go to the Guan area to survey. Qi Shouan, who once served as a defense committee member in Shandong, is the team leader. The purpose of the third survey team is to survey the tail. After the Yellow River Conservancy Commission closes the meeting in Tianjin, it will begin to organize. It is proposed that Hua Guanshi serve as the team leader. Hua is also a member of the Shandong branch of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission and is currently in Jinan. He will return to Henan after the Frost's Descent, and then lead the survey team back to Shandong. (19th)

Farmers' Riot in Suzhou 77

Thirty houses of tax collectors burned down

Local people telegraphed the province to send personnel to investigate

The issue of wasteland survey by farmers in the areas outside Loumen, Waikuatang, and Xietang in Suzhou, due to the malpractice of false reports by tax collectors, gathered more than a thousand people to carry out a riot and set fire to the houses of tax collectors. The situation has been briefly described in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that the storm was launched on the night of the 19th. More than 500 farmers outside Loumen gathered, each holding a torch, and first rushed to the house of tax collector Xing Honggao, set it on fire, and completely burned down more than ten houses in less than half an hour. Nine houses in Xing's brother Shuigen's house were also affected. Fortunately, the family escaped beforehand and was not burned to death. The farmers went to various villages to beat gongs, and in a short time, seven or eight hundred people gathered, rushed to the house of Zhu Fuchang, the deputy head of Ningnan Town and tax collector of the eighth ward of the twenty-fourth district, and burned down eight houses, with a loss of about 5,000 yuan. At twelve o'clock in the middle of the night, they rushed to Xiyi Village and demolished the houses of Wei Xiangzhou, the deputy head of Fengjing Township, and Qu Fuyuan and Qu Hengshan, the tax collectors of the twenty-eighth ward of Waikuatang, completely. At that time, the farmers were gathering more and more, and the gongs were ringing in the villages, and the fire was shining in the sky. They also went to the houses of Mao Jinan and Gao Liugen in the first ward and set fire to the houses. The crowd planned to go to the homes of tax collectors in the Guanxiduli area to set fire, but fortunately, the police district in charge sent police to block them at the Yong'an Bridge. The crowd dared not rush over and went east. Zhang Xun, an official, captured two people named Li Shouquan and Gu Lanting who were beating gongs and took them to the interrogation office. According to Li and Gu, they were both bailiffs who were forced out by the crowd to beat gongs. The two were sent to the Public Security Bureau for verification and handling. At about 2:00 a.m. on the 20th, it spread from Waikuatang to Xietang Township. Hundreds of farmers in the township also gathered and rushed to Zhu Yongxiang's house in Nanxiaozhuang to set fire, and then to the Yachengli of Qiongcheng Township to set fire continuously, burning down the houses of Shen Jinguan, Shen Heqing, and Shen Ziqing, about 20 houses were destroyed. At about 6:00 a.m., they went to Chenqidun Village in Liangcheng Township and burned down four houses of Liang Fugao, the head of the township, and five houses of the Lianghong Township. They also went to Duntou Village and demolished more than 40 houses of Yang Yisong, Yang Pinsong, and Yao Yiren. They also went to Xia Yisheng's house in Fenghui Village to set fire. In the afternoon of the same day, more than 500 farmers in Yinjia Bang Township, Huangshiqiao outside Fengmen, also set fire to the houses of tax collectors, and similar incidents also occurred in Shitan Village. On the night of the 20th, there was still firelight in the southeast of Loumen, and the authorities were investigating. After receiving a long-distance telephone report from the Xietang and other towns on the 20th, Wu, the county magistrate, immediately sent Section Chief Xu and Captain Nie to lead 20 security team soldiers to the countryside to suppress the situation and investigate the arson. After arriving in the countryside, Section Chief Xu immediately convened the villagers at Huimin Bridge and gave earnest exhortations. The villagers were quite moved and dispersed immediately. Section Chief Xu returned to the city that afternoon. The Disaster Relief Association and the various landowners first sent representatives Qian Zichu, Shen Yizhi, Shen Shie, etc. to the county government to visit County Magistrate Wu, requesting that it be effectively stopped to avoid spreading. County Magistrate Wu agreed to strictly prevent and control. County Magistrate Wu immediately ordered the water and land police teams to strictly prevent and control in the four townships to curb the unrest, and sent two security teams, led by Nie Dezhao and Zhang Dichen, to Xietang at 8:00 p.m. to stop the storm. Local people Zhang Yiju, etc., telegraphed the Civil and Financial Departments yesterday (21st), requesting that high-ranking officials be sent to Suzhou to investigate thoroughly. Wu Erchang, the head of the first district, believed that the villagers in the area outside Fengmen would also express their opinions, so yesterday (21st) he convened the heads, deputy diagram directors, town dings, etc. of Fengxi, Jingting, and other townships to hold a meeting to discuss prevention and control measures, and ordered the heads of each township to persuade the villagers not to blindly follow. In this storm, a total of more than 30 houses were burned, with a loss of about 20,000 yuan, but it is difficult to predict whether it can be quelled.

Songjiang: Poor Farmers of Cao Shitu Robbed 78

Punan Caojing is a coastal area, far from the Huangpu River. There was a severe drought in the summer, and most of the rice and cotton there were barren. Farmers worked hard all year round and it was difficult to get enough food and clothing. Therefore, the stubborn people all plotted illegitimate thoughts. The night before last, the farmer Wang Jiangshi's house in Cao Shitu suddenly came with seven or eight bandits speaking local accents, holding kitchen knives as weapons. They broke into the house through the front door and tied up Wang Jiangshi and her two young children. They searched the house but found nothing to rob. Before leaving, they robbed four bales of cotton and one cotton quilt and fled.

Wuxi: Temple Rules Muddled, Monk Hangs Himself 79

There is a Changtai Temple in Kaihua Township outside Nanmen, presided over by Monk Yuanxiu. Yuanxiu is young and frivolous, and specializes in widely accepting male and female converts outside the temple, spreading rumors to confuse the public, and making profits from it. Recently, two vegetarians, Zhu Mingfeng and Wang Zengbao, also entered the temple in the name of cultivation. Unexpectedly, they had an affair with a cooking woman in the temple who was about forty years old. The matter was known to the blind monk named Ben'an in the temple, who questioned them, but was beaten severely by Zhu and Wang. Ben'an did not dare to resist at the time, so he had to endure the silence and complained to the presiding monk Yuanxiu after he returned to the temple. Unexpectedly, after Yuanxiu heard the words, he turned around and gave Ben'an a severe beating. Ben'an was so angry with this strange grievance that he suddenly had the idea of ​​being tired of the world, so he sneaked into the room the day before and hanged himself to death with a hemp rope. It is also said to be tragic.

Salt Transport Department Bans Salt Licenses 80

The salt eaten in Jiangnan is Zhejiang salt. In the second year of the Republic of China, the county council of this county resolved to request the provincial council to transfer the advisory to the authorities to change to Huai salt. After the provincial council passed the three requests, it was in progress, but the Guizhou coup occurred and the matter was suspended. At that time, the voices of changing to Huai salt in the county were loud and clear. Yang, a native of the county, took the opportunity to obtain ten salt licenses from the salt guild and rented them to others for business, collecting a top fee of 300 yuan per license and a monthly rent of 5 yuan per license. Until the end of last month, an order was received to register sauce gardens and salt shops. The families with salt licenses must take photos of the salt licenses and send them to the Songjiang Salt Transport Department for verification. The Salt Transport Department verified that the ten salt licenses obtained by Yang had no transport imprint, and ordered a ban on business. After receiving the order, the Salt Guild is now working on canceling the ten salt licenses issued before in order to maintain merit.

Changzhou: Businessman Commits Suicide by Lying on Tracks Due to Debt 81

Dai Rongbing, a merchant and resident of Zou Xu Town, Wu County, was twenty years old. In the summer of this year, he owed a large sum of money for soybean cakes on behalf of farmers. Recently, the future was urgent to pay back. Dai repeatedly asked the farmers to pay back, but because of the drought, he could not pay for a while. Dai had no choice but to go home to discuss with his father and take the money to pay back, but he was severely reprimanded and refused to pay. Dai was extremely depressed because of this, so he went to the city early in the morning of the 20th, wrote three suicide notes and held them in his hand, and walked to the railway beside the north of the city. At about 11 o'clock, the Beijing-Shanghai express train sped past. Dai immediately jumped onto the track and lay down. In an instant, he was crushed into two pieces by the wheels, his body and head separated, and blood and flesh splattered everywhere. It was terrible to see. The town Ding there reported to the railway police section, recovered the suicide note of the deceased, and notified his family to claim the body. In the afternoon, the county prosecutor reported the case and went to examine it once. For a time, the viewers were crowded and it was passed on as a strange event.

Haimen: Bandits Rob and Injure People 85

Tang Lianhe and Feng Xianbin, residents of Zong'an Township in the Eleventh District of Nantong, were returning home from selling cotton at the Dasheng Third Factory in the county yesterday (the 19th) at around 3:00 PM. Tang shouted for help and was shot by the bandits, suffering one wound to the left leg and another to the waist. He immediately fell to the ground in extreme pain. Feng, seeing the situation was unfavorable, ran wildly to the north and reported to the Second Squad of the Third Company of the Security Forces stationed there. The squad leader, Zhou Ziwen, led all the soldiers of the Third Squad to pursue the bandits. They saw two bandits riding bicycles and two bandits walking, fleeing south. The two bandits and the stolen goods were sent to the company headquarters for interrogation. One bandit, Wang Wenkui (also known as Wang Xihui), was said to have been a detective in the county Public Security Bureau. The other, Gao Xuexun, was an unemployed vagrant in the county. Today (the 20th), they were transferred to the county government for trial.

Jiaxing: Investigation of Disaster Victims in Each District 89

Due to this year's drought in Jiaxing, many rural farmers without clothing or food have been begging from door to door. The county magistrate, Jiang Ruo, has ordered each district to investigate the exact number of affected people to prepare a relief plan and submit it for review. It is now known that the investigation of disaster-stricken households in each district has been completed, with the Fifth District being the most severely affected, followed by the Fourth, Sixth, and Seventh Districts, and then the First, Second, and Third Districts. The First District has 1,958 disaster-stricken households and 8,059 disaster victims. The Second District has 1,025 disaster-stricken households and 4,041 disaster victims. The Third District has 723 disaster-stricken households and 2,580 disaster victims. The Fourth District has 1,796 disaster-stricken households and 7,064 disaster victims. The Fifth District has 7,674 disaster-stricken households and 32,640 disaster victims. The Sixth District has 2,055 disaster-stricken households and 8,133 disaster victims. The Seventh District has 1,683 disaster-stricken households and 6,946 disaster victims. In total, the county has 68,988 disaster victims. The county government has followed the provincial disaster relief plan, dividing victims into categories of extreme poverty, poverty, and those capable of working, and has pre-determined methods such as providing porridge, selling grain at fair prices, and organizing work relief projects, which have been submitted to the province for approval.

Wang Chonghui Returned to Shanghai from Hong Kong Yesterday 91

First Met with Hu Hanmin in the South, Then Met with Various Comrades in Guangdong

All Parties Unanimously Advocate for a Combination Through Peaceful Means

According to the Central News Agency, CCP Central Committee member Wang Chonghui traveled south from Shanghai on the 9th of this month to meet with various Central Committee members residing in Hong Kong and Guangdong. In his personal capacity, he exchanged opinions on the current situation. The results were quite satisfactory. Wang left Hong Kong on the 19th aboard the Changxing Company's Canadian Empress and arrived in Shanghai yesterday at noon. He plans to rest in Shanghai briefly before going north to convey the opinions of the Central Committee members in Hong Kong and Guangdong to the Central Government. The details are as follows:

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon: Wang, accompanied by his secretary Zhu Yongshou, left Hong Kong on the 19th aboard the Changxing Company's Canadian Empress and arrived in Shanghai at 11:30 AM yesterday. The ship docked at the Gonghexiang Wharf in Hongkou. Those who came to welcome him included Tang Haian, representing the Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi; Tang Shixuan, representing Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng; former Minister of Judicial Administration Wei Daoming; former President of the Jiangsu High Court Lin Biao; Legislative Committee member Zhu Lühe; Section Chief of the Ministry of Judicial Administration Yang Kentang; former Chargé d'affaires in Paris Xie Weilun; Xiao Jinfang; Peng Sihua; and more than 30 reporters from various newspapers. After disembarking, Wang went directly to visit friends by car. He did not return to the World Academy on Fook Hing Road to rest until the afternoon.

Statement: Wang issued a written statement on the ship saying, "I originally intended to take a vacation to travel around various places in the country to broaden my knowledge. I did not want to interfere in politics. However, after returning to the country, I witnessed the increasingly dangerous state of our country and a future that is truly unimaginable. I humbly take it upon myself to fulfill the responsibility of a common citizen, and with the encouragement of friends, I have visited comrades from all sides, hoping to communicate their opinions and seek a common method of saving the country. According to my personal observation, all parties unanimously advocate for a combination through peaceful means to relieve the national crisis and turn danger into safety. This is somewhat comforting to the public." Wang also said, "During my visit to Hong Kong, I first met with Mr. Hu Hanmin. Mr. Hu expressed that although my views have differed from those of others in recent years, they were purely about matters and not about people. If the authorities can be diligent in governing, I will have no objections." Later, in Guangzhou, I had discussions with various comrades, all of whom hoped that we could meet each other with sincerity. Although our political views may differ, it is not difficult to reach a consensus. As for the details of the exchange of opinions, I regret that I cannot tell you everything. If you ask how the results will be, it all depends on the extent to which they are accepted after being conveyed. It is still difficult to speculate at this time."

Wang Chonghui, Who Returned to Shanghai Yesterday (Photo by Qichang)

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Retransmits Telegrams Protesting the Taxation of Goods from Other Provinces in Guangdong 93

Machine-Made Western-Style Goods Should Be Excluded

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly sent telegrams protesting the taxation of goods from other provinces in Guangdong Province. Recently, it was heard that Guangdong Province plans to implement it on a fixed date. The Chamber sent another telegram to the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, and Guangdong Provincial Government in Nanjing yesterday, stating: (Omitted title) Since the abolition of the Likin Bureau, according to the order of the National Government, the transfer of goods within the country, except for transit tariffs or consolidated taxes, should not be subject to any other taxes between provinces. This is an immutable rule based on tax law. Guangdong Province previously argued that it was protecting local products and planned to levy a protection tax on goods imported from other provinces. The affiliated association has repeatedly telegraphed the Guangdong Provincial Government, stating that this matter should be handled by each province in accordance with the national anti-dumping tax law and should only be levied on foreign goods, which would be more in line with the original intent of the legislation. There should be no such thing as separate territories within the same country, mistakenly using the tariff war in Europe to build barriers within the wall. If this happens, factories in the Yangtze River area will be ruined and irreparable. Once this trend starts, retaliation will follow, and Guangdong's local products will inevitably be rejected everywhere, resulting in a lose-lose situation. This has been said many times in the past. Later, the Guangdong provincial government respected the tax system, maintained domestic products, and sought ways to benefit each other. Therefore, the affiliated association also specially sent the sugar magnate Zheng Zenan to negotiate and promote the sale of Guangdong sugar in order to promote the cooperation of domestic products. Unexpectedly, according to the Hong Kong Industrial and Commercial Daily, the protection tax is planned to be levied in January of next year, and the clause exempting machine-made Western-style goods will also be cancelled. The last hope for Shanghai's domestic goods factories has once again vanished. Upon hearing this, everyone sighed. In recent years, Shanghai factories have relied on the Yangtze River and the southern provinces for sales due to domestic unrest and the war in North China. If South China hinders sales with a protection tax, the market will shrink further. Guangdong is the first to do so, and other provinces will follow suit. A province is like a foreign country. Where can factories find a place to survive? Shanghai merchants regard this as a matter of life and death for industry and cannot sit idly by. It is requested that the Executive Yuan and Ministry consider the overall situation and order the Guangdong Provincial Department of Finance to handle the matter according to the original proposal. This is fair and convenient. Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce.

Economic Expert Yu Huanzheng Discusses the Infeasibility of the Gold Exchange Standard 96

No Reason to Implement Currency Inflation

According to the Xinxin News Agency, due to the recent increase in the silver export tax, rumors are rampant, and market prices fluctuate greatly, causing public anxiety. The Xinxin News Agency reporter interviewed Yu Huanzheng, a renowned economic expert who studies gold and silver issues and is the former Deputy Governor of the Bank of China, to ask for his opinion. Yu said that he had previously advocated for increasing the silver tax and published an article on the economic supplement of the Shen Bao and the Shen Bao Monthly. Now that the government has implemented it, it is only intended to curb the export of silver. However, some people suspect that it is to change to the gold exchange standard and inflate the currency to lower its value. In my opinion, I dare to say that this will never happen. I wrote an article opposing the gold exchange standard after the Kemal currency system opinion was published, saying that it cannot be done, is not feasible, and is not necessary (There is a manuscript in the Banking Weekly and a lecture on gold and silver issues). This is such an important matter that even Kemal advocated changing it gradually by region. How can the government reform the standard recklessly without any preparation? As for currency inflation and lowering the currency value, only the United States has this method. Those who are generally unaware of the financial situation believe that our country can also imitate it. The economy of our country has not escaped the position of semi-colony. This is undeniable. I ask, before the United States reduced the gold content of its coins, it first concentrated the cash in the hands of the government. Can our government concentrate the silver stored in domestic and foreign banks one by one? If it cannot be concentrated, then it is like Dong Shi imitating Xi Shi, only to repeat the old dramas of the Bank of Communications suspending exchange and the Wuhan Hanchao banknotes. Not only will the business market be greatly disrupted, but the government's financial revenue will also be greatly reduced. Capital flight and falling public bonds are even more inevitable. How can the enlightened financial authorities be so unaware of the benefits and harms that they imitate warlords and communists to harm the people and themselves? Therefore, I dare to say that this will never happen and there is no reason for it. The current government seems to be trending towards flattening the exchange rate and stabilizing silver prices. There is already an organization of the Foreign Exchange Market Stabilization Committee, which will naturally stabilize people's hearts and the market in the future when it is effectively implemented. As for the follow-up measures after adding the silver tax, such as promoting exports to reduce imports and exports and reducing the difference between domestic and foreign silver prices to prevent smuggling, it is a long story and cannot be fully explained. The key to using it lies in the heart, and we must wait for the environment to respond to the plan. It cannot be fully explained in words.

Finance Minister Kong Denies Lowering Currency Value and Currency Inflation 97

This is Truly a Talk Without Any Financial Common Sense

According to the Xinxin News Agency, since the Ministry of Finance, based on the request of the Shanghai Silver Industry Association and others to find a way to prevent the export of silver, implemented the imposition of silver export tax on the 15th of this month, huge changes have taken place in the trading of various exchanges in the city. In particular, the gold rush has been the most significant. After the Ministry of Finance explained it once, the turmoil subsided slightly. Recently, a rumor has spread that our country will lower the currency value and inflate the currency, causing anxiety again. The Xinxin News Agency reporter went to Kong's residence on West Asam Road at 8:00 PM last night to visit Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi and ask about everything. Kong received him and said that the Ministry of Finance's imposition of silver export tax this time is intended to prevent smuggling and maintain the difference between domestic and foreign silver prices, and at the same time promote the export of domestic products in order to reduce imports and exports. As for the rumors that the currency value will be reduced and currency inflation will occur, it is completely unfounded. It should be known that our country's silver coins are scattered in the hands of the people, so how can they be reduced? This is truly a lack of financial common sense.

The Loan for Completing the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway is Issued by Two Silver Companies Through Bonds 98

Sold Abroad According to the Previous Loan Method

The Railway Bureau Will Begin Bidding and Construction Will Begin

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, the Ministry of Railways borrowed 16 million yuan from the China Construction Silver Company and the Sino-British Silver Company to complete the Chancao section of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway. The draft contract has been signed. A Xinsheng News Agency reporter learned from the banking community yesterday that after the loan is successful, the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus will begin bidding and construction will begin. The roadbed has been surveyed and the earthwork project will be started first. Except for the bridge foundation on the Cao'e River, which has already been built, the section from the Cao'e River to Shaoxing is 31 kilometers long, and the section from Shaoxing to Xixing is 47 kilometers long, with a total length of about 78 kilometers. As for the China Construction Silver Company and the Sino-British Silver Company, which are borrowing the money, they have decided to issue bonds and sell them abroad, imitating the Sino-British Silver Company loan method for the two railways. The interest rate is said to be 5%. Because foreign interest rates are mostly 3-4%, these 5% bonds are guaranteed to be reliable, and the credit of the two railways is well-known, so it is expected that sales will be good in the future.

The Wuxi Cotton Spinning Industry Appeals for Exemption from Increased Consolidated Tax on Cotton Yarn 99

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, the Chinese cotton mills have recently increased the consolidated tax on cotton yarn by the Ministry of Finance on November 1, which has exacerbated the crisis in the yarn industry and urgently needs government relief. How can we increase the burden again? Manufacturers from all over the country have telegraphed the Executive Yuan, Ministry, and Cotton Consolidated Tax Association to call for the cancellation of the previous proposal. The Wuxi Cotton Spinning Industry Association telegraphed the Shanghai Cotton Consolidated Tax Association, the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry to appeal for exemption from the increase, the original text of which reads: "I have recently heard news of an increase in the consolidated tax on cotton yarn. Roads are spreading rumors, and the industry is panicking. It has been found that the seven factories affiliated with our association, including Shenxin No. 3, Zhenxin, Qingfeng, Guangqin, Lixin, Yukang, and Fuxing, are on the verge of bankruptcy due to the impact of Japanese goods dumping and the decline of agricultural products. On October 17 of this year, they telegraphed to appeal for a reduction in the consolidated tax, but they were not approved. They were still hesitating when alarming news came that the government was instead planning to increase taxes, which is tantamount to strangling the dying. According to reports, the Chinese Cotton Mill Federation and its branches in various places have telegraphed to appeal. The factories affiliated with our association, which are located in the interior and are cotton mills in recent years, are in a depressed state and feel particularly painful. If the government really intends to increase taxes, we urge you to consider that the domestic cotton yarn weaving industry has suffered deeply and can no longer bear the burden. Please immediately cancel this proposal. Otherwise, the manufacturers' livelihoods will be ruined, and the government's tax revenue will also be reduced, which is detrimental to both. Under the pressure of the situation, the factories affiliated with our association are sending this telegram to beg you. If our request is not granted, we will have to suspend operations and await orders. In urgent hope, we respectfully ask you to consider. Cai Jian San of Wuxi Cotton Spinning Industry Association."

New Rice Successively Enters the Market, and Rice Prices in the City Rebound 100

The Top Rice is Only 11.8 Yuan

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, new rice from various places is successively entering the market, and rice prices in the city are gradually declining. The current top rice is 11.2 yuan, medium grade is 10.4 to 10 yuan, broken japonica is 11 yuan, new indica rice is scarce, and Duzi indica is 10 cents lower. Indica rice is 10.05 to 9.9 yuan, and Duzi indica is 10.03 to 9.7 yuan. According to observations by people in the rice industry, rice prices in the city this year have been affected by drought, locust plagues, floods, and hailstorms. Therefore, although new rice is successively entering the market in Kunshan, Changshu, Suzhou, and other places, the yield is not high, so it is difficult to expect a rebound. Even if there is a rebound, it will only be 10 to 20 cents.

Discussing the Affairs of Sichuan Aftermath and Bandit Suppression

Meeting with Zhang Qun and He Chengjun Under Liu's Command

As for the bandit situation on the Guizhou border, although it was tense for a time after the two bandits Xiao Ke and He Long sneaked in, the bandit forces have been sharply reduced and the encirclement has been completed thanks to the joint suppression of the armies of Hunan, Guangxi, Sichuan, and Guizhou. The bandits have lost their footing in the advance and retreat. One part collapsed towards Cheweiping, and the other fled to Xiaojing. Numerous spoils of war were seized, and the bandits suffered even more casualties. They are currently being pursued.
